Current Commentary

The First Ten Days of the Italian Army's Invasion of Abyssinia

— Hua

The Italian army launched its invasion of Abyssinia on the 3rd of this month. Today marks the full ten days. This war was inevitable, as observers had anticipated. Therefore, its formal outbreak did not cause any shock in the international community. However, the scope of this war's involvement and its final outcome have caused great concern worldwide. In the past ten days, there has been no significant development in the war situation in East Africa. In the Mediterranean and in the League of Nations, although the atmosphere is serious, there are no signs of a major change. However, the anxiety in all aspects continues to increase. Now, let us take a look at the various situations in the past ten days to observe the impact and trend of this war.

The greatest impact of this war is the blow suffered by the League of Nations. The League of Nations, with the power of the General Assembly, could not resolve the dispute between Italy and Abyssinia. Now that the Italian army has launched an invasion of Abyssinia, although the League of Nations recognizes Italy as an aggressor based on the Covenant, it may in fact be unable to implement the sanctions it should have. Most of the League of Nations' recent activities have been promoted by the power of the United Kingdom. In fact, all the League of Nations can do is formal matters. Whether its resolutions can take effect depends on the use of the military and diplomatic power of the great powers. In imposing sanctions on Italy, the United Kingdom must obtain the firm support of France. However, the result of Italian diplomacy in Central Europe is that Austria, Hungary, and Switzerland refuse to implement common sanctions. The resolutions of the League of Nations have become useless documents. It is foreseeable that the power of the League of Nations in international mediation will become weaker in the future.

The impact of this war on the United Kingdom is also not small. The Mediterranean-Red Sea route is the lifeline of the British Empire. After the power of the German-Austrian alliance was dissolved, a new threat has now emerged. Italy's tough attitude towards the United Kingdom has made the United Kingdom realize the invisible backwardness of its naval and air forces. In the future, the distribution of the military power of the British Empire in the world will probably have a major change. The United Kingdom and the Mediterranean region are of course the main force. The power in the Far East will be weaker than before. This is the layout before the Great War in 1914. The difference is that at that time, the focus was on the North Sea, and the purpose was to counter Germany. In the future, the focus will be on the Mediterranean, and the purpose will be to counter Italy. However, there is a common point before and after, that is, a compromise with Japan on the ocean in the Far East. According to a Reuters dispatch from London the other day, former British Ambassador to Japan Lintley said in a speech that the United Kingdom should compromise with Japan and not "encourage" China. Such blatant remarks are noteworthy when they are discovered now. At the same time, the impact of this policy of the United Kingdom on the world, especially on the East, cannot be ignored.

It is difficult to predict now how far this war will develop. While launching an aggression, Italy is not breaking with the League of Nations. Its purpose seems to be to prepare for diplomatic negotiations after a considerable military victory. The United Kingdom is now promoting the sanctions of the League of Nations, applying indirect pressure on Italy, while quietly watching and avoiding formal conflict with Italy. Probably, if the Italian army's aggression does not make smooth progress, and France can fully support the United Kingdom's position, then the British attitude can be strengthened and more direct intervention can be carried out. According to the war situation in the past ten days, the Italian army is not very successful. If this war is to be delayed for how many days, it will cause other important changes. Italy cannot afford long-term military expenditures. The United Kingdom cannot tolerate a long-term threat to its main routes. At the same time, the two major groups of anti-status quo and maintaining the same status in Europe are gradually becoming distinct. Once the gunpowder line in East Africa is transmitted to the Mediterranean, the entire Europe is within the scope of the explosion.

Of course, we cannot speculate too far now. Looking at the immediate aspects, Abyssinia's resistance to aggression has shown some success. This is an encouragement to the general small and weak nations, which cannot be ignored. Abyssinia, as a member of the League of Nations, should express considerable trust in the League of Nations within the possible scope. But it also knows that in order to maintain its own survival, it has to take full resistance to the aggressor. And this resistance is effective. Then, the East African war in the past ten days has already given the small and weak nations of the world a way to survive.

Italian Army's Invasion of Abyssinia Advances Towards the Southeastern Border; Shibeli River Basin Suffers Tragic Bombing; Release of Poison Gas Causes Countless Deaths and Injuries to Humans and Animals; Abyssinian Army of 100,000 Digs Deep Trenches and Builds High Fortifications to Prepare for Battle

Harar The Italian army's invasion of Abyssinia has today advanced to the Shibeli River basin in the southeastern part of Abyssinia. RShibeli bombed various villages there, and isolated Abyssinian army outposts, preparing to penetrate deeply in a major operation. The Abyssinian side has also concentrated 100,000 troops to prepare for resistance. The battle site will be on the slopes of the Wagaden Plateau, south of Qiqiqa. If Harar falls, the Italian army plans to go straight to Diridawa, cutting off the railway, and conquering Abyssinia by economic warfare. It is learned here that the Italian army's bombing in the Shibeli River basin has destroyed many villages, and has resulted in countless casualties to women and children. Refugees claim that the Italian army used poison gas, resulting in the complete destruction of humans and animals. At the same time, the Abyssinian army's front lines are also digging deep trenches and building high fortifications in preparation for a desperate resistance. (Guomin Telegram on the 13th)

Addis Ababa It is received here today that 11 Italian aircraft dropped countless bombs in the sky over Gerogubi in Wagaden Province to bomb the Abyssinian army's positions, causing great losses. Thirty-six Abyssinian soldiers hid in a cellar, and the bomb sank the cellar, causing all 36 people to be buried alive. Italian aircraft also bombed many villages in the Danakil region near the northeastern border of Abyssinia. It is heard that there were many casualties among the residents. (Reuters Telegram on the 13th)

(Rome) According to news obtained by the local newspapers, the Italian army has continued to move on the entire line in East Africa. Italian troops have continued their search in Somalia territory, and aircraft have flown to Bagerli Fortress near the Shibeli River in Abyssinia and bombed it for 40 minutes. Abyssinian chieftains in Tigray Province continue to surrender, and most tribes have also surrendered upon hearing the news. The troops led by General Sandeni, who captured the city of Hodeida, are now continuing to advance towards the eastern part of Tigray Province. According to Italian sources in Djibouti (French Somaliland), Italy is departing from Assab (in Italian Eritrea) and is advancing towards the eastern part of Abyssinia, now no more than 80 kilometers from Harar Province, which is defended by Abyssinian General Nasibu. (Havas Telegram on the 12th)

Asmara Abyssinian tribal leader Guf Chai recently fled to the Italian army. According to soldiers who fled with him, the traffic between Magal and Abyssinia has now been completely cut off. The city is believed to be the second major objective of the Italian army on the northern road, 65 miles southeast of Adua. The Italian army's northern front extends from a certain location 12 miles east of Adigrat to 8 miles north of Aksum, with a total of 60,000 troops. The Italian army is still transporting soldiers and war equipment as quickly as possible to its weak points. Soldiers on the front lines are still engaged in clearing the countryside to search for General Seyoum, the governor of the Tigray region who is hiding. The Italian army now hopes that Gugsa will surrender his people. (Reuters Telegram on the 13th)

Italian Imitation: Plotting to Establish a Puppet New Nation. Descendants of the Former Abyssinian Royal Family are Induced to Betray. Major Obstacle Removed for the Italian Army's Southern Advance from the North.

Aksimala. According to a report from our correspondent with the army, Baer, Gefchai, a descendant of the former Abyssinian royal family, has surrendered to the Italian army. Fifteen hundred of his soldiers advanced to the Italian front line, placing their guns and swords before General Tabono, a high-ranking commissioner. They shook hands and made merry with Italian soldiers outside the camp. The Italian High Command considers this an omen of military victory. Abyssinian soldiers in Tigray Province are surrendering in droves upon hearing the news. The city of Aksum has not been occupied by the Italian army but has already raised a white flag. The area around Magale is now completely under Italian control. Based on observations here, the entire Tigray Province will soon be under Italian control. (Havas dispatch, 12th)

(Rome) Official circles today openly stated that Mussolini plans to establish a new nation in at least a portion of Abyssinia, with Gefchai, the former governor of Tigray Province who recently surrendered to the Italian army with 13,000 men, as its puppet emperor. Gefchai is not related to the Abyssinian King by blood but claims to be a descendant of John IV, who ruled Abyssinia from 1872 to 1889. It is said that other important chiefs not of the Ansari tribe will soon surrender to Italy. If so, Italy will be able to control all of Abyssinia's coastal areas. The "Public Opinion" newspaper today has a headline stating, "The Legitimate Heir to the Throne Has Betrayed the Usurper in the Abyssinian Capital." The newspaper also detailed the Abyssinian royal family's lineage, claiming that Gefchai is a direct descendant of the New Solomon dynasty, while former King Menelik and current King Haile Selassie are both usurpers. It is generally believed that Gefchai's surrender will allow the Italian army to take Magale without firing a shot. (National Telegram, 12th)

(Rome) The semi-official Italian "Italian-Japanese Daily" recently commented on the surrender of Gefchai, a descendant of the old Abyssinian royal family, stating that when King Victor Emmanuel III of Italy inspected Eritrea in 1932, he met with various chiefs of Tigray Province, including Gefchai. At that time, this person requested preferential treatment from Italy and expressed his willingness to submit to Italian Prime Minister Mussolini. (Havas dispatch, 12th)

(New York) Today's most important war news is the defection of Abyssinian chief Gefchai on the Eritrean border. Gefchai has always been disobedient to the Abyssinian King. With his cooperation, the Italian army's southward advance to cut off the Ginji railway will face no major obstacles. If other chiefs follow suit, the Italian army can encircle the Abyssinian capital from the east, west, and south. Italian military personnel have been trying to induce these chiefs to surrender for months, using power and wealth as bait to make them rebel against the Abyssinian King. If Italy can induce more tribes to surrender, the time required to conquer Abyssinia can be greatly reduced, and Geneva's impatience may also arise from this. If Mussolini can occupy Abyssinia as soon as possible, the League of Nations will again have to deal with a "fait accompli." Observers believe that Britain is now in a dilemma because, on the one hand, it does not want war, and on the other hand, it cannot bear to watch the League of Nations disintegrate. Therefore, Britain's concentration of its fleet in the Mediterranean is enough to indicate that if it must engage in a war, it will strike a decisive blow. (National Telegram, 12th)

Commander-in-Chief of the Italian Army in East Africa Accepts the City of Aduwa and Presides Over the Unveiling Ceremony of the Monument

Abyssinian Capital. A telegram from Baer, our correspondent with the army, states that General Tabono, the High Commissioner of East Africa, will formally accept the city of Aduwa in the name of Italy today. All streets in the city are decorated with flowers and colored ribbons, and many triumphal arches have been erected in preparation for the welcome. General Tabono departed from the city of Koati yesterday afternoon to inspect the battlefield of 1896 (i.e., the battle in which the Italian army suffered a previous defeat) and the initial contact points at the beginning of this war, such as the Darotaikel Pass, 20 kilometers north of Aduwa. After arriving here today, he will participate in the religious ceremony held at the Koptope Church and then preside over the unveiling ceremony of the monument, which commemorates the soldiers who died in 1896. The monument is engraved with the words "The Revenge for the Soldiers Who Died in the Battle of Aduwa Has Been Avenged." After the ceremony, local chiefs will offer congratulations to General Tabono. General Tabono plans to spend the entire day on Monday studying the spiritual and material lives of the residents, as well as the local administrative and legal organization. (Havas dispatch, 13th)

(Rome) General Tabono, Commander-in-Chief of the Italian Army in East Africa, will formally enter the city of Aduwa tomorrow to take over the occupied territory. The General will hold the unveiling ceremony of the monument to the Italian soldiers who died in Aduwa in 1896 and will also be in charge of the local civil administration. The monument is a marble pillar, engraved with the phrase "October 6, 1935, the 13th year of Fascist rule, Revenge for the Soldiers Who Died in Aduwa." After the unveiling ceremony, the General will review the Second Army Corps that conquered Aduwa. (Reuters telegram, 12th)

The Italian Army Continues to Advance in East Africa: Reservists of the 1914 Class Remain in Service

(Rome) The government has recently announced an order establishing a Higher Academy of Naval Studies. The steamer "Toskano," carrying 20 officers, 320 soldiers, and some Asgari indigenous soldiers, set sail from Naples today for Messina, where it will embark 200 soldiers of the "Sila" division and depart for East Africa. Another steamer, "Piemonte," carrying 105 officers and 2,691 soldiers, set sail from Messina for the port of Massawa in East Africa. Local officials and residents went to the pier to see them off. (Havas dispatch, 12th)

(Rome) Today, the Italian government ordered reservists of the 1914 class who have completed or are about to complete their military service to remain in service pending further orders. This proves that Italy will likely not allow conscripts to be discharged while the war with Abyssinia is not yet over. (Reuters telegram, 12th)

Abyssinian Government Forces the Italian Ambassador to Leave the Country: A Special Train is Prepared to Compel His Departure

Abyssinian Capital. The government is still forcing Count Vinci, the Italian Ambassador to Abyssinia, to leave the country. If he refuses again, he will be forcibly sent on his way. According to reports, the special train prepared for him by the authorities is scheduled to depart for Djibouti at 10 a.m. (Havas dispatch, 13th)

Abyssinian Capital. Italian Ambassador Count Vinci and Lieutenant Colonel Gartliani of the Army Committee are confined to the embassy, claiming that they are unwilling to leave the embassy until all Italian consuls in Abyssinia have safely departed. This afternoon, they both "capitulated" and were escorted by Abyssinian soldiers to a fortified area five miles from the Abyssinian capital, led by local leader Taistai. Although the two will be "guests" of the Abyssinian government, they have actually been detained. After "capitulating" today, the Italian Ambassador declared that he voluntarily remained in the Abyssinian capital to await the safe arrival of all Italian consular officials from Magaro. Then he would obey the Abyssinian government's disposal. Soon after, the Abyssinian King ordered the Ambassador and Lieutenant Colonel Gartlini to be escorted to the fortified area led by Taistai. At the same time, the remaining personnel of the Italian embassy have already taken a special train to Djibouti. The soldiers guarding the Italian embassy today were all carefully selected from the army by the authorities and swore allegiance before the Abyssinian King to show their prudence. (Reuters telegram, 12th)

Abyssinian Capital. According to a report from our correspondent, Auchana, when the Italian embassy staff left Abyssinia on a special train yesterday, Second Secretary Deglena also left the station because Ambassador Count Vinci refused to depart. He was chased back by the police, who seized his pistol and pushed him onto the first train. Currently, the Abyssinian government no longer recognizes Count Vinci as the Italian Ambassador. Vinci informed the Ministry of Foreign Affairs that he wished to stay in the Abyssinian capital, accompanied by Army Counselor Colonel Gadlini, until the Italian Consul in Magalo arrives in the capital. Only force can make him submit. Yesterday, it was rumored that Count Vinci had fled somewhere, but this was found to be untrue. He is currently residing in the embassy. The Abyssinian government prohibits unauthorized personnel from entering or leaving the embassy. Only the French Vice-Consul, Temulier, is allowed to maintain contact with the Italian embassy on behalf of the diplomatic corps and to enter and leave freely. There are still several soldiers guarding the front of the embassy. A British news reporter attempted to climb over the wall to enter and investigate but was spotted by the guards, arrested, and mistreated. He was released only after receiving an imperial edict. (Havas dispatch, 13th)

The Abyssinian Army is Fully Deployed to the Front Lines: The Last Batch of 10,000 Men is Reviewed by the King. The Two Sons of the Abyssinian Ambassador to the UK Return Home to Serve

Abyssinian Capital. Our special correspondent, Auchana, declared that 10,000 Abyssinian soldiers were reviewed by the King in front of the palace yesterday. They then marched in formation through the streets, singing war songs. Previously, the Abyssinian King issued a general mobilization order, ordering all conscripts nationwide to enlist before October 12. Those reviewed yesterday were the last batch. Many troops have been sent to the front lines in recent days, and the capital has become deserted. (Havas dispatch, 12th)

(London) The eldest son of Dr. Martin, the Abyssinian Ambassador to the UK, 23 years old, and the second son, 22 years old, are scheduled to return home on Tuesday to rush to the front lines and join the air force. (Havas dispatch, 12th)

League of Nations Committee Discusses Sanctions Against Italy: Eden Asks Member States to Boycott Italian Goods. French Experts Do Not Advocate Overly Harsh Measures

(Geneva) At yesterday's meeting of the Committee of Seventeen to discuss economic sanctions against Italy, British representative Eden urged member states to implement a ban on Italian exports as the third type of sanction against Italy, stating that League of Nations member states purchase 70% of Italy's total exports. If these sales are cut off, the effect will be significant. If League of Nations member states further ban the export of certain major products to Italy, the effect will be even greater. This ban will undoubtedly cause inconvenience to League of Nations member states, but it can be reduced through mutual assistance. Economic pressure can also be implemented by stopping the supply of food necessary for Italy to wage war, but this must be done with caution and will take a longer period of time to achieve. Eden also urged the prompt implementation of various effective sanctions. French technical experts supported Eden's view on banning goods from entering and exiting Italy, but said that while the opportunity for reconciliation has not been completely lost, sanctions should not be overly harsh and suggested that the Committee of Seventeen should currently focus on banning the transport of major products to Italy. Romanian representative, Foreign Minister Titulescu, suggested that it is now appropriate to examine how to reduce the economic losses suffered by the countries boycotting Italy. Representatives from South Africa, Belgium, the Netherlands, and the Little Entente all enthusiastically supported Eden's points of view. It is now hoped that when the Committee of Seventeen reconvenes on Monday, the recommendations made by Eden can be fully discussed. Yesterday, all three subcommittees held discussions on the implementation of sanctions against Italy. The financial subcommittee's proposal to halt all financial and commercial lending activities to Italy seems to have little practical relevance because lending transactions have already ceased since the Italian government implemented currency control regulations. The Third Committee is currently discussing whether other items can be added to the list of prohibited war materials being transported to Italy. (Reuters telegram, 13th)

Russian Representative Suggests Restraining Those Who Hinder Sanctions

(Geneva) The 17-nation subcommittee of the Sanctions Plan Adjustment Committee recently held a meeting to discuss various measures to enable non-member countries to economically cooperate in suppressing Italy, but no decision was taken. Soviet representative Potemkin advocated imposing financial and economic restraints on countries that refuse to implement Article 16 of the Covenant, namely: (1) The debt that these countries can raise shall not exceed their usual needs. (2) The exports of these countries shall not exceed the amount of previous years. It is generally believed that the Soviet Union's proposal is aimed at Austria, Hungary, and Albania. Other non-member countries that hinder sanctions are also included. British representative Eden put forward the following suggestions: (1) All member states of the League of Nations should refuse to import Italian goods. This measure could affect 70% of Italy's exports. (2) Raw materials and products that can be used for war industries should be prohibited from being transported to Italy. In addition, he proposed that each member state quickly compile a list of goods being transported to Italy and submit it to the Secretary-General of the League of Nations so that a detailed list can be prepared. (Havas dispatch, 12th)

Mexico Joins the 16-Nation Subcommittee

(Geneva) Because Mexico has a large oil production capacity, the Sanctions Plan Adjustment Committee recently elected a representative from that country to join the 16-nation subcommittee, becoming the 17-nation subcommittee. The Financial Issues Subcommittee organized by the subcommittee (consisting of the UK, France, Greece, South Africa, the Netherlands, Poland, and Romania) elected former Greek Foreign Minister and honorary governor of the National Bank, Maximus, as chairman. Other national representatives include the British Undersecretary of the Treasury, Hordley, the Polish economic advisor to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Wiczlacki, and the Romanian Minister of Foreign Affairs, Titulescu. (Havas dispatch, 12th)

Close Cooperation Between Britain and France: Military Sanctions Have Not Been Mentioned Yet

French Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval recently told our reporter in Clermont-Ferrand that cooperation between Britain and France continues unabated, and they have taken the same position in the League of Nations.

Page 6

The guarantee stated, "During my meetings with British cabinet members, this issue has not been mentioned" etc. (Havas dispatch, 13th)

(London) The Constitutional Club held a closed-door meeting today. Ten people unanimously passed a resolution urging the government not to advocate or participate in any sanction plan that may lead to war. The meeting was chaired by Emmeli, the former Minister of the Colonial Department and successor Minister of the Dominions Department. (North China Daily, 11th exclusive)

Austria's Position: Unwilling to Sell Out a Friend

(Vienna) The semi-official political news agency recently explained that Austria is a loyal member of the League of Nations, but the measures taken by the League of Nations have the nature of punishing a great power, and this great power, in Austria's most difficult and challenging times, held a firm and unwavering attitude and provided Austria with effective assistance. Even in the most superficial terms of loyalty, Austria has to make some reservations. If Austria were to repay the most valuable and sometimes most practical assistance with malice, it would inevitably lose the sympathy of the world, including the British people. In particular, Britain values reputation the most; would it want to see Austria sell out a friend? (Havas dispatch, 13th)

The Second International Supports the League of Nations

Brussels. The Second International recently held a meeting here to discuss the Italo-Abyssinian dispute. It passed a resolution stating that it was satisfied with the League of Nations designating Italy as an aggressor, and stated, "The Second International will certainly provide practical assistance to any sanctions that the League of Nations may decide on with the aim of stopping the war between Italy and Abyssinia and quickly restoring peace. This is what the Second International can guarantee to the League of Nations." The resolution also requested the League of Nations to decide on sanctions and implement them in a short time, so that the Italian government would realize that the results that it can obtain through acts of aggression are no greater than those that it can obtain without engaging in war. After the resolution was passed, the representatives unanimously decided to telegraph a summary to the President of the League of Nations General Assembly, Czech Foreign Minister Benes. (Havas dispatch, 13th)

Britain Induces Cuba to Participate in Sanctions

Havana. The British Ambassador to Cuba recently met with Secretary of State Bauerney and indicated to him in a semi-official manner that if the Cuban government can support the attitude held by Britain in the Italo-Abyssinian dispute, then Britain will assist Cuba in commerce as an exchange. Bauerney replied, "Cuba will take the attitude of the majority of the League of Nations as its attitude," but declined to explain the country's implementation of sanctions against Italy in the future. (Havas dispatch, 12th)

Germany Takes a Reserved Attitude: Implementing Economic Blockades Will Cause Great Losses to Various Countries

(Paris) The Paris Echo reported that German personnel in Geneva issued a statement last night stating that the German government does not intend to decide on any position regarding the Italo-Abyssinian dispute. Neither the League of Nations nor Britain invited Germany to participate in the Sanctions Plan Adjustment Committee. It said, "Germany will adopt a reserved attitude. It will separately study any sanctions that the Adjustment Committee may recommend after they are announced." The "Business Daily" stated that according to information obtained by a correspondent in Geneva for the Austrian semi-official "Federal Post," Italian Prime Minister Mussolini is about to put forward three suggestions in the hopes of resolving the Italo-Abyssinian dispute: (1) The Italian government will be entrusted with ruling the three Abyssinian provinces of Harare, Hargaden, and Tigray. (2) Italy will undertake not to attack the Abyssinian capital with aircraft. (3) Peace negotiations will be held through the League of Nations. (Havas dispatch, 13th)

(Berlin) The Evening News recently published a long article explaining that countries participating in sanctions will suffer significant sacrifices. It stated, "We know the meaning of an economic blockade very well. (Note: Germany was subject to an economic blockade during the European War.) The sacrifices suffered by a country fighting to maintain its right to survival due to economic starvation are extremely significant. Italy's needs for coal, timber, oil, rubber, and various minerals are almost entirely dependent on foreign countries. In addition, Italy's exports have recently decreased significantly. The number of foreign tourists visiting Italy has also decreased. All of these factors are enough to prove the difficulty of Italy's position. However, if other countries impose economic sanctions on Italy, then they themselves will inevitably feel a great loss. Taking Yugoslavia as an example, its exports to Italy account for about 20% of its total exports. Romania exports a large amount of oil to Italy. Once sanctions are implemented, these countries will inevitably be the first to feel the impact." (Havas dispatch, 13th)

Fascists and Opponents Fight Fiercely in New York: Clubs and Glass Bottles Fly, Leaving Many Injured with Broken Heads and Bloodshed

(New York) Thousands of fascists and anti-fascists fought fiercely this morning, using clubs and glass bottles as weapons. When mounted patrols arrived to suppress them, many people had broken heads and were bleeding. Today is Columbus Day, and there is usually a celebration ceremony in Times Square. When Mayor Chardia and Governor Limen finished their ceremony and left the venue, the riot suddenly broke out. Both sides punched each other, and glass bottles flew in the air. Large teams of mounted patrols were quickly called to the scene to suppress the violence, but many people were already injured. (Reuters telegram, 13th)

Amidst the Italo-Abyssinian War, American Prices Skyrocket: Industry and Commerce are Poised for Huge Profits

(New York) The most important factor in the US economic situation this week is the danger of credit inflation. Gay, the president of the New York Stock Exchange, expressed his opinion on Wednesday that if the government does not stop it soon, the stock market may experience a dangerous surge. The new chairman of the Federal Trade Safety Commission, Landis, said that the commission does not have the necessary power to stop the surge in market prices, and the government does not intend to take other measures to control the activities of the exchange beyond those that have already been implemented. After the above statement was released, the prices of various unstable securities on the exchange were stimulated and rose sharply. In view of this, the government did not include raw materials in the list of goods prohibited from being transported to warring countries. The market prices of various raw materials subsequently rose, reaching heights not seen since May 1930. In addition, the general trend in various industries is generally good, which is also one of the reasons for the rise in raw material prices. Because the American people believe that the Italo-Abyssinian war will be limited in scope and will not expand, American industry and commerce can reap huge profits. In short, the general economic situation in the United States is similar to that in mid-August, with the only difference being that the activity in heavy industry has slightly decreased. (Havas dispatch, 12th)

Three Near East Muslim Countries Sign Non-Aggression Pact: Persia, Turkey, and Iraq

(Tokyo) Ambassador Okamoto in Iran reported to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs on the 11th that the non-aggression treaty between Iran, Turkey, and Iraq was concluded and signed in Geneva on the 10th. (Japan United Press telegram, 13th)

Japan Develops the South Seas: A Ten-Year Plan is Proposed: A Colonial Development Company is Established with Funding of 30 Million Yen

(Tokyo) The South Seas Research Committee met on the 12th and decided on a ten-year plan to develop the South Seas and its funding of 30 million yen. The Nanyo Development Company, which is the center of the plan, will be capitalized at a total of 20 million yen by the Toyo Takushoku and Nanyo Development Companies. The Ministry of Colonial Affairs will contribute a phosphate ore area (which can produce 60,000 tons of phosphate ore per year). (Japan United Press telegram, 13th)

US and Japan Reach a Gentleman's Agreement: Restricting Japanese Cotton Fabric Imports to the Philippines, Conditioned on the Philippines Not Increasing Tax Rates

(Washington) Negotiations between the United States and Japan on the issue of restricting Japanese cotton fabric exports to the Philippines have been ongoing for a long time. Recently, a gentleman's agreement was reached, stipulating that from September 1 of this year, Japanese cotton fabric exports to the Philippines shall not exceed 45 million square meters per year. In the past twelve months, the total amount of foreign cotton fabric imported by the Philippines was 95 million square meters, of which 60 million square meters were imported from Japan. The current agreement limits this to no more than 45 million square meters. In addition, State Department officials also plan to restrict the import of Japanese cotton fabric into the United States in the same way as the Philippines, and are currently studying it. (Havas dispatch, 12th)

(Washington) It was announced here today that Japanese exporters have agreed to limit sales of cotton fabrics to the Philippines to 45 million square meters per year for two years, starting from August 1 of this year, on the condition that the Philippines does not increase tax rates. In 1934, Japan's sales of cotton fabrics in the Philippines reached 56,356,000 square meters. State Department officials stated today that after careful consideration, they believe that this limit will benefit the cotton fabric industries of both the United States and Japan and will not harm the interests of the Philippine people or impose any responsibility on the Philippine government. It is said that "the governments of the United States and Japan have completely agreed that this approach can avoid increasing conflicts between the two countries' business communities due to excessive competition and can solve economic difficulties and protect legitimate interests." The agreement also stipulates that the limit can be reduced by up to 10% in any one of the two years and transferred to the limit of another year, but it may not exceed 26 million square meters in any six months. The State Department stated that if calculated by value, the United States' cotton fabric exports to the Philippines under the new agreement will be about double that of Japan. In the first eight months of this year, Japanese cotton fabrics accounted for 57.7% of the entire Philippine market, while American goods accounted for only 37.7%. (National Telegram, 12th)

日偽軍挑釁　侵入俄境開槍射擊　蘇聯向日嚴重抗議

(Moscow) According to today's Manchurian news, a small detachment of Japanese-Manchu soldiers, totaling fifty men, crossed the Russian border near Grodekovo, not far from Khabarovsk, and opened fire on Russian border guards. The Russian soldiers returned fire, reportedly resulting in several casualties. According to the government news agency, the Soviet Russian government has instructed its ambassador in Tokyo to lodge a firm protest with the Japanese authorities. (Reuters, November 11)

(Moscow) The government formally announced today that Soviet Russian and Japanese troops had engaged in clashes on the Manchurian border in recent days, resulting in casualties on both sides. It is claimed that on October 6, 8, and 12, Japanese troops had violated the Soviet Russian border, leading to exchanges of rifle and machine-gun fire. The Soviet Russian government has lodged a protest with the Japanese government and proposed the dispatch of investigators to clarify the facts of the conflict. (Guomin News Agency, October 13)

(Tokyo) Regarding the issue of the Soviet-"Manchukuo" border commission, Mr. Nishi Haruhiko, Chief of the First Section of the European and Asian Bureau of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, who had been in Manchuria for about a month to ascertain the views of the Kwantung authorities and investigate the actual situation on the ground, returned to Tokyo on the 11th. Yesterday, he reported everything to Foreign Minister Hirota and Director-General Togo of the European and Asian Bureau and held lengthy discussions. As a result, "Manchukuo" has adopted an opposing attitude towards establishing the commission, arguing that it is premature. Therefore, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has decided to hold a conference of the three ministries—Foreign Affairs, Army, and Navy—next week, focusing on Mr. Nishi's report, to study the matter further. The Foreign Minister will then convey "Manchukuo's" views to the Russian Ambassador. Consequently, pessimistic sentiment surrounding this matter is quite strong. (Dentsu News Agency, October 13)

(Tokyo) According to a public telegram from Ambassador Ota to the Soviet Union addressed to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Counselor Sakako and Far Eastern Minister Kazinovsky held negotiations on the revision of the Japan-Soviet Fisheries Treaty on the 10th, but there was no progress. The Japanese side repeatedly insisted on abolishing the auction system and, in accordance with Article 2, Section 2 of the treaty, allocating fishing zones in the form agreed upon by the Japanese and Soviet governments, as well as extending the period for stabilizing fishing zones. The Soviet Union reserved its response to these two points until the next meeting. (Dentsu News Agency, October 13)

五强　海軍會議　數星期內江在倫敦召集　美官塲料未必有何結果

Five-Power Naval Conference to be Convened in London Within Weeks; American Officials Expect No Results

(Washington) According to reliable sources today, a naval conference has indeed been scheduled to take place in London within a few weeks, although the opening date has not yet been determined. At the same time, naval experts from both Britain and the United States are still seeking input from the Japanese navy. It is widely known that American officials feel deeply that this conference will ultimately yield no results. They believe that, being bound by existing treaty constraints, they have no choice but to attend. (Guomin News Agency, October 12)

波瀾新閣成立　前內障任總揆

New Cabinet Formed in Poland; Former Minister of Interior Appointed Prime Minister

Warsaw: Following the resignation of the Sławek cabinet yesterday morning, President Mościcki entrusted the task of forming a new cabinet to the outgoing Minister of Interior, Gościarz Wóycicki. The cabinet has now been announced as established. Apart from the changes in the ministers of Finance, Commerce, Interior, Education, and Public Welfare, the remaining ministers have been retained from the previous cabinet. These include Deputy Prime Minister and Minister of Finance, Kwiatkowski, Minister of Commerce, General Gorecki (formerly the President of the National Bank), and Minister of Interior, Raczkiewicz. The newly appointed Prime Minister, Gościarz Wóycicki, is a native of Vilnius, 43 years old, and one of the young colonels of Poland. He participated in the Polish independence movement and joined the famous "Revival Corps" organized by the late General Piłsudski. In 1918, when the Polish independence army entered Warsaw and disarmed the German garrison in the city, Gościarz Wóycicki played a significant role. From then on, he gradually rose to prominence. In 1920, during the war between Poland and the Soviet Bolshevik Party, Gościarz Wóycicki distinguished himself even further. In 1922, he was elected as a member of the House of Representatives, originally belonging to the left wing of the Peasant Party. (Havas News Agency, October 13)

比與英日電台合作　環球播音成功　歷程八萬四百公里　僅需時一分四十秒

Belgian Radio Cooperates with British and Japanese Stations; Successful Global Broadcast Covering 80,400 Kilometers in Just One Minute and Forty Seconds

Beijing: The Belgian General Directorate of Posts has recently cooperated with wireless radio stations in Britain and Japan to conduct a long-distance broadcast. The journey covered 80,400 kilometers and took only one minute and forty seconds, setting a world record in both distance and speed. The broadcast originated from Beijing, passed through New York City in the United States, Montreal City in Canada, Sydney City in Australia, London in the United Kingdom, Buenos Aires City in Argentina, Tokyo in Japan, Beirut City in French-mandated Syria, and returned to Beijing, circling the world twice. (Havas News Agency, October 13)

美參院調查委會　研究購銀政策　主張白銀恢復本位　俾於對華貿易有利

U.S. Senate Investigating Committee Studies Silver Purchase Policy; Advocates Restoring Silver Standard to Benefit Trade with China

Salt Lake City, USA: The Senate Committee Investigating Government Silver Purchase Plans today studied the impact of silver purchase policies on import and export industries. Those present included Senators Pittman, Borah, King, William, Thomas, as well as the Secretary of the Senate Foreign Relations Committee, Hyde, and the Director of the Foreign Affairs Division of the Department of Commerce, Jones. The committee reported on U.S.-China trade. It is said that Senators Thomas and Borah both advocated for immediately restoring silver as the U.S. currency standard at a price of $1.29 per ounce. Senators Pittman and King, however, expressed satisfaction with the current plan. Senator Thomas strongly asserted that silver should be restored as the standard currency while Congress still has the power to do so, fearing that a change in government might lead to the abandonment of the silver policy. Senator Thomas also stated that if silver is not a fundamental monetary metal, it is merely a token. As for China, after the rise in silver prices, it has been able to purchase more foreign goods without harming Chinese commerce. Foreign investors in China only see that rising wages and prices will reduce their profits. Foreign banks also oppose the rise in silver prices because it will reduce the value of their Chinese securities holdings. However, Americans, when considering the interests of others, should first protect American interests. Senators Borah, Pittman, and King made no statements. Senator King only mentioned that the results of the investigation would be published next January. (Guomin News Agency, October 12)

蘇聯海軍勢力　軍事費膨脹積極造艦

This year's figure has reached 6.5 billion rubles. Consequently, the number of warships newly built within the scope of naval power is also substantial.

Youngest Son of Exiled Spanish King Marries in Rome Church

(Rome) Prince Juan, the youngest son of the exiled Spanish King Alfonso, who is considered a potential heir to the throne, married the Countess of Marchesi of Sicily today in the largest church in Rome. There were 7,000 guests, mostly Spanish aristocrats. The women all wore red and yellow (the colors of the Spanish coat of arms) carnations in their hair or held them in their mouths. The exiled king will host a grand banquet tonight, inviting 2,000 guests. After the banquet, the newlyweds will go elsewhere for their honeymoon, the location of which has not been announced. 北寗路機車出軌　到平各車誤點

Beining Railway Locomotive Derails; Trains Arriving in Beiping Delayed

(Beiping) At around 3:00 AM this morning, extra train No. 101 from Beiping to Tianjin derailed its axle at around 5:30 AM in the Hankouzhen area west of Yangcun, and one of the cars overturned off the tracks. Upon receiving the news, the Tianjin Main Station urgently dispatched a repair train. The repairs were completed at around 8:00 AM. Trains to Pukou, Shenyang, and Shanghai from Beiping were all delayed. The Beiping-Pukou train was delayed by three hours, the Beiping-Shenyang train by two hours and seven minutes, and the Beiping-Shanghai train by one hour and nineteen minutes. (Special Dispatch, October 13)

(Tianjin) At 4:00 AM on the 13th, extra train No. 103 on the Beining Railway, from Beiping to Tianjin, derailed its axle at the Yangqiwai outside of Hankou East Station. The carriages connected to the rear were also dragged off the tracks and tilted. The rails and sleepers were all damaged. All trains to and from Beiping and Tianjin were blocked, and traffic was cut off. Upon receiving the report, the Railway Bureau immediately dispatched a repair train for repairs. After moving the derailed cars to the side of the road, traffic was restored at 9:00 AM. Trains to Shenyang, Shanghai, Pukou, and Yulin from Beiping were all delayed for about three hours before departing from Tianjin. (Special Dispatch, October 13)

News on Preparations for Newspaper Paper Factory

(Nanjing) The location of the newspaper paper manufacturing factory has been re-surveyed and determined to be Mawan on the north bank of the Zhenjiang River. Commercial shares are currently being negotiated. The construction plan and budget drafted by the Ministry of Industries have been submitted to the central government and will be approved soon. Construction will then begin. The machinery has been ordered from the United Kingdom and consists of complete turbine generators, which can be shipped to China next spring. (Special Dispatch, October 13)

律師恊會　積極進行寃獄賠償

Lawyers Association Actively Pursuing Wrongful Imprisonment Compensation

(Nanjing) After the draft law on wrongful imprisonment compensation was passed by the Judicial Conference, the Lawyers Association submitted the draft to the Legislative Yuan, where it has been referred for review. The association believes that the number of people in the country who have suffered wrongful imprisonment and the loss of life and property are staggering and will be shocking if thoroughly investigated. Therefore, implementing wrongful imprisonment compensation is the most important task of the new judiciary. The association has sent a circular to all local lawyers' associations, requesting them to investigate local cases of wrongful imprisonment and report them to the association within a specified time limit in order to forward them to judicial organs as a reference for eliminating the long-standing malpractices of the judiciary. (Special Dispatch, October 13)

收回廬山英租借地　將開始估計英人財產

Reclaiming the British Concession in Lushan; Valuation of British Assets to Commence

(Nanjing) Jiang Zhicheng, the director of the Lushan Administration, came to Nanjing on the 13th and will meet with President Wang in the coming days to report on the progress of the draft agreement for reclaiming the British Concession in Lushan. He received a telegram from Lushan urging him to return to Lushan immediately. Mr. Jiang is scheduled to fly to Xunyang on the 14th morning and then to Lushan. After the matter is completed, he will return. Mr. Jiang stated that after the Lushan Concession is reclaimed, it is planned to be turned into a national park. It is also learned that the issue of reclaiming the concession in Lushan, under the instructions of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, was negotiated by Jiang Zhicheng and the British Consul-General in Hankou, Mershon, over a period of 14 months, resulting in a draft agreement last month. The content of the agreement stipulates that all concession areas will be unconditionally returned to China. The ownership of the land originally belongs to China, and any fixtures that were originally owned by the concession authorities will also be taken over by the Chinese side. Currently, both the Chinese and British sides have hired accountants to audit the assets of the British in the concession and will jointly audit them on the 20th of this month, which is expected to be completed in three or four days. This will facilitate the future payment of house taxes and land rents by British nationals. Both sides will sign the agreement in Lushan around the 25th, with Mershon representing the British side and Jiang Zhicheng representing the Chinese side. After the agreement is signed, an advisory committee will be formed, whose nature is only advisory. There will be four Chinese members and three British members. The term of this committee is seven years. The Administration will be responsible for all administrative matters, and the advisory committee cannot interfere. The organization of the Administration will consist of three sections and will not be expanded. For important design projects, personnel will be transferred from central, provincial, and municipal agencies. All persons residing in Lushan in the future must comply with all Chinese laws and pay house taxes and land rents. If they fail to pay for two full years, their property will be unconditionally taken over as public property. However, those who return to their home country may pay five years of house taxes and land rents in advance, otherwise, they will be treated in the same way. (Special Dispatch, October 13)

范予遂抵京　報告南潯路路務

Fan Yusui Arrives in Nanjing to Report on Operations of the Nanxun Railway

(Nanjing) Fan Yusui, the director of the Nanxun Railway, arrived in Nanjing and met with Gu Mengyu, the Minister of Railways, on the 13th to report on the railway's operations. He is scheduled to go to Shanghai in one or two days to discuss the signing of a joint transportation contract between the Nanxun Railway and the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. Fan stated that the road work on the Yushan-Nanchang section of the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway has been underway for more than two years since construction began. The entire road surface and tracks have been laid, and preparations for opening to traffic are being made. It is expected to be realized by the middle of next month. The entire section is over 300 kilometers long and cost over 18 million yuan. Vehicles will temporarily not need to be purchased when traffic opens. Jurisdiction belongs to the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Company. Once the Cao'e River Railway Bridge is completed, transportation between Nanjing and Jiangxi will be directly accessible. The Zhushao Railway project is also expected to be completed next year. The Guangdong-Hankou Railway project is also progressing rapidly, and the completion date should not be far off. As for the business conditions of the Nanxun Railway, since the banditry in Jiangxi Province was quelled, passenger transport has shifted to freight transport, which should gradually increase in the future. The total Japanese debt of the Nanxun Railway is 10 million yuan, and one-third has been repaid. The remaining debt repayment and interest payment plan has also been agreed upon, with the Railway Bureau designating the funds to be paid monthly. The purpose of my coming to the Ministry is to report on the railway's operations. I am scheduled to go to Shanghai within days to meet with Liu Hongsheng, the director of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, to discuss the joint land and water transportation contract between the Nanxun Railway and the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. The content principles were previously agreed upon and are generally the same as those of other railways. The trial period is two years. (Special Dispatch, October 13) The Ministry of Personnel is planning to register diplomats to facilitate personnel qualifications, as the number of foreign embassies and consulates has increased annually, and the number of diplomatic personnel has increased accordingly. It has already begun drafting registration regulations and will implement them after submitting them to the Executive Yuan for approval. (Special Dispatch, October 13)

Xigong Banner Dispute, Compromise Solution Agreed Upon, Awaiting He Jingwu to Go North to Handle, Mongolian Political Council Will Also Submit for Discussion

Beiping Correspondence: Regarding the Xigong Banner dispute between Mongolia and Suiyuan, although it has once entered a serious situation, the path to a peaceful resolution seems not to have been cut off, due to the belief on both sides of "not making things worse". The third plenary session of the Mongolian Political Council opened on the 9th of this month. Because the commissioners were not all present, the discussion was postponed. However, on the future meeting, there will inevitably be important resolutions on the Xigong Banner issue. What extent will the future development be, is worthy of attention. The key to resolving this issue is no longer in the Suiyuan and Mongolia sides themselves, but in how the central government handles it. When the news of the central government sending senior officials north to thoroughly investigate the case reached them a month ago, the Mongolian side informally expressed the hope that the central government would appoint trusted Mongols to serve, otherwise it would only complicate the situation. Its meaning is nothing more than rejecting consultants related to Suiyuan officials in this matter. As for the inside story of the case, both Mongolia and Suiyuan have issued telegrams. Oqiguang, deputy director of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission's office in Beiping, once ran around to mediate, but the result was nothing. Recently, since the central government decided to send He Jingwu to take charge of handling this matter, in addition to preparing to make a resolution at the third plenary session, the Mongolian side also seems to be eager for the central government to quickly mediate, so there are several people mediating everything between Suiyuan and Bailingmiao so that He Jingwu can smoothly resolve it when he goes north for a thorough investigation. The final compromise solution is estimated to be (1) the Beizi title of Shi Wang will still be retained, (2) the Zhasake position of Xigong Banner will be entrusted to someone else. The Mongolian side has agreed to accept it, and the transfer of personnel is currently soliciting opinions from the Suiyuan side. According to the Suiyuan authorities, all measures taken by the province against Mongolia completely comply with the orders of Taiyuan, so it is necessary to convey the opinions of the Shanxi provincial authorities. As far as the current situation is concerned, if the Shanxi provincial authorities can handle this compromise solution accommodatingly, then the Xigong Banner dispute can be said to have no problems. Once He Jingwu comes north to handle the legal procedures, Lang can completely resolve it. According to this, a telegram from Beijing recently stated that He Jingwu's trip north has been delayed due to illness. However, if the mediation of the Xigong Banner case is smooth, and both Mongolia and Suiyuan can accept the method of transfer, then He is also willing to travel with illness. Wu Heling, a member of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission, arrived in Beiping from Beijing yesterday (October 10th) to attend the third plenary session of the Mongolian Political Council. According to his statement to others, the Xigong Banner dispute is not difficult to resolve, but how to eliminate the gap between Suiyuan and Mongolia after the resolution, he is very willing to discuss at length. Wu made great efforts to mediate the issue of the Suiyuan Mongolia special tax in the previous time. Therefore, this trip to Bailingmiao will also engage in mediation in a personal capacity. (October 12th)

Hebei Province, River Defense Faces Major Danger, Lengzhai and Other Places above Liuzhuang May Breach, Jiangsu and Shandong Will Still Be Affected If It Breaches Again

Jinan Correspondence: The Dongzhuang breach blocking project on the Yellow River in Shandong Province has been implemented on schedule. Unexpectedly, alarming news came that Lengzhai in Hebei Province was facing a major danger due to changes in the river's course, and the situation was serious, and it was feared that it would follow in Dongzhuang's footsteps, which is quite alarming. The reason is that Lengzhai, more than ten miles above Liuzhuang in Hebei Province, is about fifty or sixty miles away from Dongzhuang in Shandong. Recently, because the Yellow River's course has been raised, the main stream directly hits the south bank embankment. The second section of the south bank, up to Tianhezui, is about three kilometers long. On the 11th of this month, it breached towards the trench. The upper part of the fourth section to Xiaolengzhai is more than one kilometer long, and the river beach continues to collapse. The dam in the area is thin and the soil is loose, and the water surface is two meters higher than the ground. By the 12th, the river beach at Tianhezui had been washed away by thirteen or fourteen meters and is still collapsing. The willow bottom brick dam between the sections of Xiaolengzhai in the fourth section of the south bank has come into contact with the side stream, and the critical situation has reached its peak. There is a shortage of funds and materials, and it is feared that it will not be preserved. Qi Shouan, Director of the Hebei Provincial River Affairs Bureau, has been on the job supervising and rushing for seven days, and the situation has not improved. Chen Yasan, the magistrate of Shan County in Heze, also rushed to the site for inspection on the 11th. Because of the critical situation, if measures are not taken quickly, not only will Hebei Province be unfavorable, but Shandong and Jiangsu will also be affected. Qi Shouan asked Chen Yasan for assistance due to the shortage of funds and materials. Chen has already sent a telegram to Han Fuju, Chairman of the Shandong Provincial Government, and also telegraphed the Breach Blocking Association and the River Affairs Bureau for a report, requesting instructions on everything, and requesting the Hebei Provincial Government to take measures quickly. After receiving the report, the provincial government has approved it and sent a telegram to Shang Zhen, Chairman of Hebei Province.

Yuehan Railway, Zhushao Project Progresses, Most of the Entire Project is Completed, Pingle Section Opened to Traffic at the End of Last Month

Guangzhou Correspondence: Except for the southern section of the Yuehan Railway from Guangzhou to Shaozhou and the northern section from Changsha to Hankou, which have already been opened to traffic, only the Zhushao section has not been fully laid. Therefore, the construction of this section is actively underway. The Zhushao Road project is divided into three small sections: the section in Guangdong Province is from Lechang to Pingshi, the section in Hunan Province is from Leiyang to Hengzhou, and the section from Hengzhou via Zhuting to Zhuzhou. Most of the entire project from Lechang to Zhuzhou has been completed. Earth and stone works have been completed by 89%, tunnels have been completed by 80%, large bridges have been completed by 64%, small bridges and culverts have been completed by 83%, and track laying accounts for 44% (177.6 kilometers have been laid). It is expected that the Zhushao Road will be fully opened to traffic by the end of next year. As for the small section from Lechang to Pingshi, it started operating on September 20, officially selling tickets, and passenger and freight traffic is quite prosperous. The train times and fares for this section have been stipulated as follows: The train departs from Lechang at 7:00 a.m., arrives at Qimen Station at 8:28 a.m., and the fare is 40 cents (calculated temporarily at third class). It departs from Qimen at 8:38 a.m., arrives at Luojiadu Station at 10:00 a.m., and the fare is 80 cents. It departs from Luojiadu at 10:05 a.m., arrives at Pingshi at 10:32 a.m., and the fare is 95 cents. The train returns from Pingshi to Lechang, departing at 3:30 p.m., arriving at Luojiadu at 3:57 p.m., departing from Luojiadu at 4:02 p.m., arriving at Qimen at 5:24 p.m., departing from Qimen at 5:34 p.m., and arriving at Lechang at 7:02 p.m. The departure times of each station are connected with the Guangshao section of the Yuehan South Road. The joint transportation between the Guangshao section and the Leping section was scheduled to be implemented on the Double Tenth Festival. Agreements have been made on joint transportation regulations and passenger and freight fares. After the implementation of joint transportation between the two sections, passengers and goods can go directly from Guangzhou to Pingshi, in other words, directly to the border of Hunan, which is more convenient for transportation between Guangdong and Hunan provinces than before. As for Hengzhou Station in Hunan Province, it is the center of the Zhushao section and a second-class large station of the Yuehan Railway. The station was built in April 1934 and completed in August of this year. The Zhushao Road Bureau has already moved in to work. The surrounding venues, roads, vendor shops, and staff residences are being completed in order. Therefore, the road bureau also held the official opening ceremony of Hengzhou Station on the Double Tenth Festival. (October 9th)

Suijing Department of the Third District of Fujian Arrests the Chen Weijin Faction, Chen Organizes the Black-Clad Gang Throughout Several Counties

Xiamen Correspondence: This time, the Fujian Provincial Government and the Suijing Department recruited all the local armies in the province without restrictions and forgave the past. However, the bandits who refuse to be recruited and continue to do evil will be thoroughly suppressed. Chen Weijin, a notorious bandit from Quanzhou and a former subordinate of Chen Guohui, a native of Matou, Nan'an, was the only one who refused to be recruited. He nominally disbanded his bandit troops, collected his firearms, and organized the so-called "Black-Clad Gang". Taking Chen's hometown of Matou District in Nan'an as the center, he recruited local soldiers, disbanded bandits, hooligans, and academic scum into the party. The party members were densely distributed in several counties of Nan'an, Yongchun, and Anxi, with great momentum. Chen Weijin himself claimed to go to Tokyo, Japan, to study this spring, but left his confidant Chen Shijin in Nan'an to preside over the work and still be directed by Chen Weijin, burying military fire and secretly transporting weapons and ammunition, plotting wrongdoing. The Suijing Department, upon receiving the report, ordered Li Yannian, commander of the Suijing Department in the Third District, to search and disband them. Li ordered Xie Fusan, commander of the 26th Brigade of the Ninth Division, to personally lead a thousand men from the 51st Regiment and more than 300 men from the 9th Security Regiment, to spread out in Matou District in the early morning of the 6th at 3:00 a.m., from Nanpu in the south to Jiudu in the east, Yuangiaoling in the west, and Dabapu in the north, taking a large encirclement of the villages in Matou District, searching Jiudu, Kuzhu, Tangbian, Kutian, Gechun, and other villages from 3:00 a.m. on the 6th to late at night on the 7th. A total of more than 20 people, including Chen Weijin's mother Chen Lei, Chen Weijin's third concubine Lin Xueyu, who had just been sent back from Japan, Chen's sister-in-law, Chen's confidants Chen Shiwen, Chen Bing, Chen Qian, and Chen Zhen, were arrested. Chen Shijin escaped, but his mother was arrested. Also, male and female teachers of the Central Primary School in Matou, who were suspected of being members of Chen's party, were arrested. After interrogation, they were released on bail. A certain member of the Incense and Paper Donation Bureau was also suspected of being a member of Chen's party and was detained for strict interrogation. At the same time, in Chen's mother's hometown, a large cannon was unearthed, in a very new style, which was purchased from Germany by the former Chen Guohui, worth 30,000 to 40,000 yuan. After Chen's family members were arrested, they were escorted to the 20th Brigade Headquarters, and Brigade Commander Xie personally interrogated them. Chen's mother volunteered to be responsible for handing over all the firearms hidden by her son, and then ordered Lei Jinpi to lead the way, and a gun-making machine was found in Jiudu, which could make machine guns and rifles, and the scale was very large, which was rare in Fujian Province. Also, fifteen boxes of bullets were found in Xialiao, and two cannon wheels and a mortar were unearthed in Kutian. As for the rest, Chen's mother said she did not know where they were hidden. When Chen's family members were arrested, Chen's mother entrusted Chen Pingqing, who had previously served as the magistrate of Yongchun County under Chen Guohui and is now the manager of Quanzhou Yongde Automobile Company, to plead with Brigade Commander Xie. Brigade Commander Xie ordered all the hidden guns to be handed over at noon on the 8th, and ordered Chen Weijin and his party members to rehabilitate themselves, and then Chen's family members would be released. Chen agreed, but failed to fulfill the agreement on the scheduled date, and then requested a three-day extension. From the 9th to the 11th, the deadline for handing over the weapons was still not fulfilled. Now three requests for extension have been made, until the 14th. If the hidden weapons are still not fully handed over by the deadline, Chen's family members will still be dealt with. Currently, Chen's mother, Chen Shijin's mother and wife, and other important party members are all banned in Jiudu and heavily guarded.

Songjiang Builds Branch Line, Dongmen Strikes

After Songsi Road was opened to automobile traffic, construction began on a branch line connecting with Songhui Road, about two li long, passing through a section of Dongwai Market Street. Local gentry and businessmen previously believed that it would hinder the prosperity of Dongwai Market, and petition representatives continued to travel back and forth, appealing repeatedly. Magistrate Jin had repeatedly promised to temporarily suspend work and wait for the provincial government to issue instructions. However, the workers continued to step up their work. Yesterday, piles were driven in the Dongmen Market River to build bridges. Merchants and residents felt that the market had been divided into two and could not be maintained. Now, it even blocks commercial transportation, believing that there is no hope for business operations and that the demolition of houses is too much of a sacrifice. They telegraphed the province to fight for their rights and automatically went on strike yesterday. After the local gentry reported to the county government, Magistrate Jin ordered the director of the Public Security Bureau, the district chief of the first district, and several standing members of the Chamber of Commerce to rush to persuade them and at the same time remove the piles to open up the transportation. Then they resumed business. Now, the local merchants and residents have telegraphed the provincial government again, requesting the dispatch of personnel to inspect and listen to a normal solution.

New County Magistrate's Definite Date of Taking Office

The newly appointed County Magistrate Li Leng recently telegraphed his friends here, saying that he will arrive in Songjiang by early train on the 15th to take office. The county government is speeding up the handover work so that it can be handed over on time. Hou Mingen, the former chief of the Second Section, has been ordered to transfer to the Chuansha County government. There will be major changes at that time.

Suzhou, Construction Bureau Approves Continuation of Road Widening

The Wu County Construction Bureau has completed the project of widening the streets in the east, west, and middle markets inside Changmen. However, the problem of the sidewalk has not been resolved because the entire business community there firmly requested to lay cement. Director Zhou of the Construction Bureau recently accepted the request of the business community on the road outside Changmen to continue widening the section of the street from the Changmen city gate through the drawbridge to the Yuyudun to Shilu Intersection and rebuild the Changmen city gate to facilitate transportation. He immediately drafted a plan and project budget and submitted it to the Construction Department for instructions. On the 13th, he received instructions from the Construction Department for approval and must start construction within the year. After the streets are widened, cars can go directly from the road to the east, west, and middle markets in the city, which greatly facilitates transportation and is of great importance to the development of commerce.

Wuxi, Anti-Smoking Inspectors Arrive in Wuxi for Spot Checks

In order to investigate the recent anti-smoking situation in various counties, the Department of Civil Affairs specially sent Inspector Wu Jichen to inspect the counties along the Jinghu Road. After receiving the order, Wu arrived in Wuxi the day before yesterday. Yesterday morning, he went to the county government to meet with County Magistrate Wang and stated his intentions. Secretary Xia Dingwen accompanied him to inspect the county drug rehabilitation center and the prison branch. In the afternoon, he continued to go to various opium dens and smoking houses to conduct spot checks. Once the work in Wuxi is completed, he will go to the Suzhou-Changzhou area for inspection.

Changzhou, Requesting to Stop Collecting Business Tax on Behalf

The Wuyi County Chamber of Commerce held a joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees on the afternoon of the 12th, chaired by Xu Juxi, and resolved important cases: (1) The floods in Jiangbei were severe, and the chamber should promote fundraising to relieve the disaster victims. It was resolved that in addition to separate fundraising by various industries, advertisements should be placed in newspapers to solicit donations. (2) The brokerage firms collect business tax on behalf of the government. Zhejiang Province has now canceled it. It is proposed to telegraph the Ministry of Finance to follow the example of Zhejiang and quickly order the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance to stop collecting the tax to alleviate the difficulties of businesses. It was resolved to pass it. (3) The Shanghai National Goods Promotion Association came to Changzhou to hold a national goods exhibition. A letter was sent to the chamber and the Federation of Trade Unions to discuss borrowing a venue. It was resolved that the local industrial and commercial groups are preparing for a national goods exhibition. The chamber will jointly reply to the association with the Federation of Trade Unions, asking them to postpone their visit to Changzhou.

Yangzhou, Preparing for Autumn Firefighting Review

This county has received a notice from the provincial capital to hold a firefighting exercise and review competition this autumn. The Public Security Bureau convened a meeting of the heads of various fire brigades in the city and suburbs at 2:00 p.m. on the 12th. More than 30 representatives from more than 20 fire brigades, including Xiangshan and Quanan, attended the meeting. Yao Yuncong, chief of the Second Section of the Public Security Bureau, chaired the meeting. Seventeen detailed rules for the review were resolved to be held on October 20 in accordance with the provincial capital. Members from various fire brigades will be organized to prepare everything in advance with the Public Security Bureau.

Construction Bureau Limits Demolition of Houses for Bridge Repair

The Jiangdu County Construction Bureau believes that the Kaiming Bridge east of Siwang Pavilion in the old city is located in a key transportation area, but it has been in disrepair for a long time. For the sake of tidying up the city appearance, it has formulated a development plan, planning to demolish the houses on both sides of the bridge to widen it. It has now drawn up a plan and submitted it to the Construction Department for instructions. The Construction Department has approved the construction of a flat bridge. The County Construction Bureau has notified the Public Security Bureau, which has notified twelve shops next to the bridge to move out within two months.

Opium Offender Flees, Recaptured and Shackled

Lu Naixiang, a resident of Touqiao Town, the third district of Jiangdu, was detained by the county government for privately smoking opium and handed over to the Political Police Office for custody. Unexpectedly, at 8:00 p.m. yesterday (11th), Lu actually escaped from custody, lifting the iron wire of the skylight net in the patio. Later, the police on duty, together with the police chief, checked the number of people and called Lu's name but received no response. The entire team patrolled for days, dispatched to various city gates to check. Chasing to the Huoqiao wharf, Lu was about to board the Datong steamer to Shanghai. He was immediately arrested and reported to County Magistrate Ma, who instructed him to be shackled and strictly dealt with.

Nantong, Turmoil in the Native Cloth Market Unresolved

The establishment of the Nantong Native Cloth Market, which centralizes cloth merchants to collect cloth, strictly stipulates standards, and cracks down on fraud, was mistaken by weavers as hindering the cloth market, causing a crowd to destroy it. After the opening ceremony on the 12th, the weavers broke in again. After the military and police suppressed it, the crowd dispersed. However, on the way, Wang Songtao, an employee of the market, was suddenly kidnapped and rescued by the police team at Yaogang. Thirty-eight people were arrested on the spot and sent to the County Public Security Bureau together. More than a thousand weavers entered the city to petition the county government, and the shops closed one after another, causing great chaos. All the military and police were dispatched, but the weavers insisted on demanding people from the county government. The soldiers opened fire to warn them, but it was ineffective. The bullet injured a weaver, Ni Sigehai, who was sent to Nantong Hospital for treatment after being examined by the court. The 38 people arrested were released on bail by Xu, the chief of the first district, at 7:00 p.m. that evening. The weavers then agreed to return home. The special commissioner's office and the county government believe that the purpose of the native cloth market is to promote rural sideline occupations and develop foreign trade. The weavers have not been able to understand it. In addition to the publicity by the heads of townships and villages, the native cloth market is ordered to open as usual.

Jiaxing, Minor Disputes Lead to Homicide

Wu, the wife of Pei Jinfu (a mason), a resident of the west end of Sanbu Liangpan Bridge in Wangdian Town, Jiaxing, used to set up a stall in front of her door to sell vegetables. Unexpectedly, at about 10:00 a.m. on the 12th, a certain wife of Zhou Wu Mao, a tofu maker, passed by the vegetable stall, and two small foreign coins fell to the ground. Wu actually stepped on them, causing a dispute. At the same time, Pei Jinfu helped his wife Wu beat Zhou's wife severely, even with fists and feet. Zhou's wife was injured and fell to the ground, unconscious. After someone informed the Fifth Public Security Branch, the police arrested the two murderers (Pei Jinfu and his wife Wu) and tried to find a doctor for treatment, but she did not wake up. By evening, her limbs were icy, and she had only a breath left, and her life was feared to be unsalvageable.

Holding Training Course for Township Chiefs

嘉xing County Government once considered the heads and deputies of rural towns as cadres for promoting county administration, with very significant responsibilities. All heads and deputies of rural towns throughout the county have been carefully reviewed by the county government and rewarded or punished accordingly. Currently, a training session for heads and deputies of rural towns is being organized. The plan has been drafted by the Civil Affairs Section, and the training is scheduled to begin on October 21st, lasting for seven days. The training methods include lectures, discussions, practical exercises, and individual interviews. The training subjects cover the county's administrative overview, Baojia laws and regulations, air defense knowledge, international situation, and the essentials of the New Life Movement. Additionally, health check-ups will be conducted. The county magistrate will soon instruct all heads and deputies of rural towns to comply and report on time for the training.

Hangzhou: Malaria Epidemic Along the Southern Yushan Section

The Hengfeng-Yiyang section of the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway's Yushan section was originally a lair of communist bandits. Since the bandits were suppressed, corpses have been left in the mountains and fields, a ghastly sight, and impossible to bury. As a result, a type of virulent malaria suddenly appeared after autumn, spreading rapidly. Over four hundred of the five hundred or so railway workers in that section have contracted the disease, and many have died. In recent days, the number of local residents who have died is about one hundred. This has greatly affected the track-laying project, causing it to be significantly delayed. The Railway Bureau has dispatched doctors with a large supply of medicine to treat the patients. In recent days, this malaria has spread to the Yushan area and efforts are underway to eradicate it.

Ningbo: Grand Welcome for Archbishop Cai

The Papal Delegate to China, Archbishop Cai of Ningbo, is stationed in Beiping. This time, he went south to inspect church affairs in various parts of Jiangnan. Wherever he went, he was warmly welcomed. Archbishop Cai, along with his secretary Yu Bin and Lu Bohong, arrived in Ningbo on the Xin Ningshao steamer from Shanghai on the 11th. Upon receiving this telegram, various agencies in Ningbo and the Catholic Church on the north bank of the Jiangbei River erected colored arches to welcome him in front of the church door by the pier. Earlier, they had sent representatives to Shanghai to personally greet the archbishop. When the Xin Ningshao arrived at the port at 6:30 am on the 12th, representatives from various agencies and churches boarded the ship to welcome him. At that time, firecrackers were set off and military music was played. Archbishop Cai, led by Bishop Dai, disembarked and boarded a car, with military music leading the way. Welcomers lined the docks and proceeded in an orderly fashion to the Catholic Church on the north bank of the Jiangbei River to attend Mass. At noon, the garrison commander Wang Haonan, Commissioner Zhao Cisheng, County Magistrate Chen Baolin, Police Chief Yu Jimin, Court President Wang Bingyi, Standing Committee member of the Party Headquarters Wu Zemin, Chairman of the Chamber of Commerce Yu Zuochen, and others held a public banquet at the Chamber of Commerce.
