Spring and Autumn

Snippets

— (Ma Gang)

There are two kinds of women in the world: one, only others perceive her good qualities; the other, only her husband perceives her good qualities. You can find ten out of a hundred women who only others perceive her good qualities; you can hardly find one out of a hundred women who only her husband perceives her good qualities.

A poet is someone who sees what others cannot see; he cannot see what others can see; he can think of what others cannot think of; he cannot think of what others can think of; he cannot do what others can do; he can do what others cannot do.

Shao Zonghan said: "The most painful thing is when you have to laugh when you don't want to; the most ridiculous thing is when you have to cry when you don't want to; the most terrifying friend is the one who is funny when you don't want to laugh; the most sickening friend is the one who is crying when you don't want to cry; a friend who can't laugh or cry is a happy castaway."

The Path to China's Economic Improvement (Continued)

— Yu Huan Cheng

6. A Concrete Outline in Imagination I

How should my ideals be implemented? This is very complex and profound. It is difficult to explain clearly in a short time. Let me briefly, very briefly, talk about the general outline in concrete terms:

(1) The vast majority of farmers are the sole target for economic improvement.

(2) To improve rural areas, industry should be integrated with agriculture, using local industries as a byproduct of agriculture.

(3) Vigorously restore the water conservancy projects that have historically existed.

(4) Extremely promote research in agricultural chemistry.

(5) Existing light industries should be controlled and subsidized; seek improvement through maintenance rather than expansion.

(6) The state should use its utmost power to establish heavy industries; all heavy industries should be state-owned.

(7) Strive for material self-sufficiency and avoid repeating the mistakes of mercantilism.

The following will provide a brief explanation of each item.

7. Explanations for Items (1) and (2)

Establishing the country through agriculture, establishing the country through industry; these have now become a focal point of discussion on China's economy. Mr. Peng Xuepei advocates: "60% agriculture, 40% industry." Agricultural and industrial progress together (see "Social and Economic Monthly," Volume 2, Issue 5) is a more reasonable approach. I believe that agriculture and industry should not be too clearly separated. Except for heavy industries, which should have specific locations and specialized workers, other light industries can all be used as rural work and agricultural byproducts. I am not copying Kropotkin's old articles on "factory, farm, and workshop"; I have very strong reasons. Integrating industry with agriculture may seem too novel, and yet too outdated. Listeners will certainly suspect that it violates the modern meaning of division of labor and the principles of large-scale centralized production, and reverts to the phenomena of the handicraft era. This is a misunderstanding. I advocate integrating industry with agriculture because I am confident that it is most suitable for the object of China's economy and in line with the latest world trends. The reasons are:

(A) Chinese farmers have too little arable land. According to statistics from the Legislative Yuan: "In 25 provinces, 58 million farming households cultivate an average of 21.5 mu of land per household. Based on five people per household, each farmer only gets a little over 4 mu of land." And the investigation report of the Zhejiang Civil Affairs Department states: "Farmers in Zhejiang occupy 1.9 mu of land per person." Arable land is already so narrow. Among them, tenant farmers account for 31% of all farmers (according to the "Shen Bao Yearbook," reprinted from the survey of the Central Agricultural Experimental Institute in the 23rd year of the Republic). The land they cultivate is not their own. One can imagine their poverty. Not only can large-scale actions such as mechanized farming not be discussed, but even the very small capital for improving soil seeds is not easy for farmers to raise. Without promoting industrial sideline occupations of agricultural products, rural areas cannot be relieved.

(B) There is little arable land, and the population is large, so farmers have surplus idle time. According to estimates by Professor J.L. Buck of Jinling University: "Farmers can only work 80-90 days a year, and almost three-quarters of their time is completely wasted." Our country does not have machine horsepower to calculate, and even manual labor has strength but no place to sell it. Especially rural women, whose original weaving has been abandoned. Except for giving birth to children and cooking, there is nothing to do all day long. Only a very few places still have women's work such as silk weaving, mat weaving, straw hat making, and lace making. Most rural women are simply outside of productive work. Those who eat are many, and those who produce are few. How can they not be poor! Without finding a way to integrate industry with agriculture, there is no way to use farmers' idle time, and there is no way to enable rural women, who account for half of the population, to engage in productive work.

(C) Find ways to utilize natural power. Wind power, water power, so that scientific utilization and mechanization extend to the countryside. In the countryside, there were old water-powered rice mills and paper mills. The mechanical group was clumsy, and the effectiveness was not great. The use of wind power is extremely rare. In all places where there is no electricity, methods should be devised locally to make full use of natural power. The cost is light, and there is no need to purchase from outside. Starting from simple scientific machinery, the rural atmosphere is opened up. Naturally, farmers will slowly take the road of using scientific machinery. I once thought that in windy places on the coast and in the mountains, wind power could be used to generate electricity and store it in storage batteries for gradual use. When there is no wind, work will not stop. I heard that Soviet Russia already has this method (see "Scientific China," Volume 5, Issue 1). It coincides with my ideal. I hope that electrical engineers will do their best to research. If it works, electrification across the country will be easier to achieve. Steam engines and hydropower generation are very costly. At the beginning, it is especially difficult to use all the electricity. Wind power generation may be a simple way to promote electrification.

(D) Gradually change handicrafts into small mechanical industries, and change domestic industries into small factories. The economic system of the family gradually integrates with modern material civilization. The small diesel engine mill mentioned above is a good example.

(E) The capital of rural small factories may be raised by investors or loaned by the government. The essence of cooperation should be used. In addition to capital interest and worker wages, there are also profits, which are limited to improving or expanding the business of the factory or local public use. It is necessary to achieve production by using goods and not production for making money, so as to avoid the poisonous effects of capitalism spreading to the countryside and causing competitive and fraudulent thinking habits.

(F) Small factories do not harm the principle of division of labor. The original production of each rural area is different, and the products of small factories naturally vary accordingly. They can be exchanged with each other, implicitly containing the meaning of division of labor. It is not "one person's body, prepared by a hundred workers." However, extremely industrialized factories, even a single screw or iron bar, can cause workers to work for a lifetime, turning them into machines, with no sense of being a living person. This is something that rural factories do not have.

(G) For factories with a wider range of products, the government should divide several rural areas into one region; and set up a model factory in a more central location. The purpose of this factory is not to compete with small factories for profit, but to plan ways for small factories to improve and to make them imitate. Because each factory scattered in rural areas cannot understand the world's new inventions and the changes in transportation and sales at any time. This model factory researches and invents, and guides them at any time on how to improve so that the manufactured products are not backward and inferior. The model factory is the mentor of each factory in the region. If a method of improvement is invented, or the guidance to each factory is very developed, the government will give special rewards. In this way, although the factories are separated and scattered, they still have a spirit of unity and no disadvantages of being scattered and backward. As for the joint transportation and sales of each factory, and sales cooperation, of course, it is a proper meaning, and the government should plan and guide it early.

(H) Modern large-scale production and centralized management are nothing more than making products excellent and costs low. However, because of capital profits, competition has led to overproduction, causing a world panic. Bankruptcies and unemployment have been going on for four or five years, and there is still no clue. (The so-called economic improvement at this time is due to the vigorous repair of war preparations in various countries and the great development of military industry; it is not that the panic has been reduced. One can understand this by looking at the world's trade statistics and the situation of various disputes in the United States.) Those who ask for industrialization must not read dead books and follow the wrong path of others. Moreover, the situation mentioned above cannot be followed at all. If the factories are scattered in rural areas and guided by model factories, the products may not be very good, but they will not be decadent. Raw materials are taken locally, and the cost is naturally low; farmers use spare time and unemployed rural women to work, and wages are naturally low; rural eating, drinking, and living are more frugal than in cities in all aspects, and expenses are naturally saved. The four characters of low cost can be achieved without large-scale production. To resist the cheap dumping of imperialism, I am afraid this is the only way. We cannot use Gandhi's hand-spinning machine to resist British goods, but setting up rural factories and exchanging products everywhere may also achieve the same effect as Gandhi.

(I) The establishment of rural factories should be handled by local governments, who should recruit knowledgeable and experienced talents to establish a "Agricultural and Industrial Economic Committee." Based on the local situation, the types of industries should be selected, capital should be raised, and the collection of raw materials and the transportation and sales of products should be specified, and the people should be persuaded to handle it. At the beginning, the scale may be simple and small, and the investment should be light. As long as you take this road, it will naturally gradually develop.

The reasons mentioned above for integrating industry with agriculture are mostly from a positive perspective. From a negative perspective, let's talk about preventing abuses.

(J) Now, in the era of three-dimensional warfare and the prevalence of air attacks, destroying resources is the primary task of attacking the enemy. If all factories are set up in large cities, and our national defense is not fully equipped, just a few large bombers can sweep everything clean in a few hours. How dangerous is this? If the factories are scattered in rural areas, the enemy will not find a concentrated point for bombing, and naturally, they will be much safer. Even if several places are bombed, it is not a total loss.

(K) Labor-capital disputes are inevitable after the development of industry. Italy's professional group method cannot be imitated by our country for a while (mentioned above). Only by using cooperative methods to run rural factories, the factory owners and workers are all one, and there is no distinction between labor and capital, so how can disputes arise. This is the best way to avoid labor-capital problems caused by capitalism.

(L) Urban factories often invest hundreds of thousands to millions. When it's good, it's a tool for profit; when it's bad, it all becomes scrap copper and rotten iron. In the environment we are in now, without national power to protect us, and with the economic imperialism pressing so urgently, the chances of failure are greater than the chances of success. Even if we are fortunate enough to encounter an opportunity (during the European War), it is only for the extravagant pleasures of a few capitalists. If we fail unfortunately, with our country's capital being so weak, it will cause financial panic. Unemployed workers have no money for food and clothing, which is even more pitiful. Wandering in the city, it is inevitable to brew danger. The road of capitalism has not yet been taken, and the abuses of capitalism have all been received. Rural factories only invest thousands to tens of thousands. Failure in several places will not have a major impact. The workers are originally farmers who lack sideline occupations and live a little worse, but there is still agriculture to retreat to, so they will not wander without a home. For the epidemic of panic and unemployment, rural factories can be regarded as a kind of vaccine.

(M) "Reviving the countryside" and "returning to the countryside" are the most fashionable slogans at the moment, but talents are still crowded in cities. The vanity of aiming high and the comfort of fearing labor and suffering certainly make a group of young people unwilling to serve in the countryside. However, the countryside only has old-fashioned agriculture, which is too monotonous and cannot accommodate talents. On the one hand, the countryside is not short of outstanding talents, but simple agriculture binds them, making them have no opportunity to practice and improve, burying many talents. If factories are set up everywhere in rural areas, those who go to the countryside will not only be useful for those who study agriculture, but also for various scientific talents. And smart talents in the countryside also have the opportunity to practice industry and science, so that talents are not crowded or buried. The problem of college students' careers may be solved in this way. However, I very much hope to bring the knowledge of the city to the countryside, and I am extremely afraid that the extravagant and lazy customs of the city will harm the countryside. Various disinfecting prescriptions must also be prepared in advance.

(8) Explanations for Items (3) and (4)

Integrating industry with agriculture and rural factories have been said so much, but it only gives farmers more opportunities to work, and makes factories a sideline for the people. It does not talk about the problems of agriculture itself. Agricultural problems are naturally complicated, and the most important and urgent thing is the water conservancy project, which has been passed down for thousands of years and is called the Asian mode of production by European scholars. From the ditch system to the guiding of rivers, large and small are not left out. Historically, great achievements have been recorded. Since the corruption of the Qing Dynasty's politics and the civil war that has lasted for more than 20 years in the Republic of China, the most glorious page of our nation in history, water conservancy, has been abandoned and not discussed. Every year, there are floods and droughts, and every year, there are famines, which have trapped the vast majority of farmers in the country in a desperate situation. Those who starve to death starve to death, those who commit suicide commit suicide, and those who flee flee. Saving the dying and helping the wounded cannot be done, so how can we talk about construction and development. The integration of industry with agriculture and rural factories mentioned above, under that state, is the same as Emperor Hui of Jin's saying to give meat to a hungry people, it is all nonsense. Until recently, the government has gradually paid attention to water conservancy. Opening canals in Shaanxi and Sui and dredging the Huai River in Jiangsu have seen some achievements, but due to insufficient funds, the plan has been reduced and reduced, and the project has been reduced and reduced again. On the one hand, there is much talk about water conservancy, and on the other hand, there are great floods, droughts, and famines, forming an extremely contradictory phenomenon. Of course, water conservancy projects cannot be completed in a short period of time, nor can they be effective in a short period of time. However, the government's allocation of water conservancy funds is too small. Within the budget, there is no special water conservancy fund. Only several hundred thousand to several million are allocated from the cotton and wheat loan (allocated to the Economic Commission for construction projects) within the relief fund, and the rest are pushed to the local government to complete the matter. Last year, the Central Political Conference resolved to unify the administrative case of water conservancy, with the decision that "in the general budget, starting from the 23rd year of the Republic of China, an annual central water conservancy project fee of 5 million yuan will be listed, which will be claimed and managed by the Economic Commission on a monthly basis." With our country's land being so large, the number of waterways being so many, and the abandonment of water conservancy being so long and far away, what can be done with a mere 6 million yuan? The Jianghuai River transport can cost almost tens of millions as soon as it moves. The government will not say water conservancy if it does not say it. If it says water conservancy, it will never be a trivial matter to deal with casually. It must make a great determination, raise great funds, and start great work to make the rural areas across the country see some results. All kinds of public bonds have been issued a lot, but there is not a single bond for water conservancy, which is the economic foundation of the whole country. When it comes to water conservancy, issuing 100 million or 50 million public bonds is not too much. Because this is completely profitable. Moreover, every basket, every hoe, every piece of wood, and every stone are mostly taken from within the country, and there is no need to purchase foreign goods. If we use 500 million or 100 million to do water conservancy on a large scale, without corrupt people inserting themselves in it, seeking truth from facts, then when construction starts, millions to tens of millions of disaster victims can be supported. After the project is completed, tens of millions of hectares of arable land can be opened up, and agricultural production can be increased by one or two times. The minimum limit is to eliminate or reduce the current disasters by more than half. Can't the 500 million or 100 million public bonds recoup the capital? In other words, other public bonds are not suitable for issuance, only water conservancy public bonds can be issued. Without water conservancy in place, the 30 million farmers, who account for the largest part of the country's population, have no way out. It is already obvious that the country's agricultural products are not enough for the country's use. It is a pity that we have nothing else besides agricultural products. And when will we be able to create other things? I'm afraid the days are gone. In addition to water conservancy, we should first stabilize the rural foundation before thinking about improvement methods. What else can be done?

If we can do water conservancy on a large scale, the arable land will naturally increase, and agricultural production will naturally increase. However, during this period of national seclusion, as long as agricultural products are sold a little more, people will be jealous. The United States started planting tung trees, and in the British Parliament, there were several accusations against my export of egg yolks, whites, and meats. Even if we increase production, if we have more than enough for our own use, and exchange goods with others, we will either lower the value or restrict the quantity. Lowering the value is indirectly squeezing our labor. Restricting the quantity is to make our products unable to be exchanged. We possess these surplus agricultural products in vain, just like American farmers using wheat to feed livestock, or like Brazil burning coffee. Producing more but not being able to use it still cannot improve the lives of farmers and solve the poverty of farmers. Our goal is not to commercialize agricultural products, but to achieve self-sufficiency and improve our living standards. If agricultural products are commercialized, the lives of ordinary farmers must rely on international trade. If other countries have panic or war changes, we will suffer. The historical failure of sericulture is a lesson in the commercialization of agricultural products. Not only is my country not striving for success, failure is inevitable. Even Japan, which once dominated for a while, has suffered the pain of falling silkworm prices. They boast that weaving is the national vein, but ultimately the vein of weaving cannot withstand it, and they must seek another lifeline. We must not envy the commercialization of agricultural products, this unreasonable development. Instead, we must increase our own production and improve our own lives.

Agricultural products are simple, unlike industrial manufactured products, which are convenient for daily use and endless enjoyment. How can we improve our lives with simple agricultural products? Then we must rely on agricultural chemistry.

Dr. William J. Hale of the United States: "Natural mineral deposits will eventually be exhausted. All kinds of raw materials used in a country's chemical factory can abandon mineral deposits, oil wells, and other natural sources, and obtain them from agriculture. In the future, agriculture will definitely not only be able to supply food like it is now. A large part of the agricultural products must be engaged in Synthetic Chemistry, using crops as raw materials to supply us humans with all the materials for daily clothing, housing, and construction, as well as fuel and other necessities."

Dr. Hale cited the example of Internal combustion Engines being modified to burn alcohol. Internal combustion engines only need to change the carbon compound restrictor and mix 10% or 15% of pure alcohol in ordinary gasoline to increase the combustion power of gasoline. Alcohol is made from starch, and corn, which contains the most starch, can extract 30 pounds of alcohol per bushel. The remaining 26 pounds of residue are still good feed for livestock. The total amount of alcohol produced in the United States each year is about 100 million gallons. If 10% alcohol is added to gasoline, 1.6 billion gallons will be needed. The current number of alcohol manufacturing plants must be increased more than tenfold, and the raw material corn must also be increased to 700 million bushels. If 50% alcohol is added to gasoline, the United States will need 4 billion bushels of corn each year, which is more than twice the current corn production in the United States. It is only feared that it is not enough, why should it be too much.

This is to find a way out for surplus agricultural products. However, the United States produces the largest amount of gasoline in the world. Using more alcohol will inevitably reduce the use of gasoline. Oil merchants will definitely object. Dr. Hale's views may not be entirely suitable in the United States, but they are most suitable in China! My country currently does not produce gasoline. Water, carbon, and alcohol are being tested. And some people have invented artificial gasoline using vegetable oil and other raw materials, which is also being tested. If alcohol can really be used as a substitute for gasoline, then we can widely plant potatoes and other raw materials, which can produce more than American corn. Studying alcohol production to make the price of alcohol lower than gasoline will not only have countless benefits in transportation and industry, but also make national defense much more secure.

In addition, the manufacture of artificial rubber and bakelite also requires agricultural products. Various agricultural chemical manufacturing experiments that will be successful include using corn stalks to manufacture alcohol, and using similar raw materials such as rice bran, bran, etc., Xylose and other agricultural wastes to manufacture fuels and coal gas. AlphaCelulose is extracted from sugarcane dregs. The United States Department of Agriculture's Industrial Agricultural Production Division assists in using straw and sugarcane dregs to make building and insulating boards for commercial use (all of the above are from the 14th and 15th issues of the 12th year of the Rural New Report). Agricultural chemistry is currently the most important thing in the United States, and it is changing with each passing day. As Dr. Hale said: All kinds of raw materials in factories are taken from agriculture. In the future, perhaps this new fact will be judged. Our country must catch up, there must be agricultural chemistry, and then the increase in agricultural products can improve our lives. And then rural factories will have meaning.

9. Inventions for Items (5), (6), and (7)

The above has explained the general direction. If we can really do this, in three or five years, the lives of farmers will gradually stabilize, and rural factories will have a clue. Can our country's economy be considered to have embarked on the road to improvement? Still not. Because modern countries are competing too fiercely, a country's economy must achieve self-sufficiency to be considered complete. In peacetime, it can exchange resources, and in wartime, it can be self-sufficient. If my country builds rural factories on a large scale, the factory machinery and refined raw materials (such as chemical drugs) must still rely on people. We are still far from self-sufficiency. The strength of a country and the foundation of national industrialization all lie in heavy industry. My country's heavy industry can be considered non-existent at all (not paying attention to heavy industry but advocating industrialization is a characteristic of my country's foreign doctors). In peacetime, we can still rely on imports, but when something happens, there is no way at all. Regardless of the needs of agriculture or industry, there is no place to settle. However, the small-scale farming agriculture in the country requires very few mechanical raw materials, so it is relatively unimportant. Light industry lacks the supply of heavy industry products, and it is difficult to operate. If the diesel engine has no diesel, the engine becomes waste. If the machine has no steel parts, the machine becomes waste. A country without heavy industry cannot talk about industrialization. Even the rural factories mentioned above have an unstable foundation. To achieve self-sufficiency, the first step is to relieve the vast majority of farmers, and the second step is to establish heavy industry. The two can be carried out simultaneously. As for the existing various light industries, they are desolate and scattered, and most of them are struggling on the line of death. To investigate the reasons for their decline: let's put aside the internal diseases, such as backward technology, mismanagement, and shortage of funds, for the time being, and focus on the external situation. Foreign pressure accounts for about 70%, and the decline of rural areas accounts for 30%. Because most of the domestic consumers are farmers, when the farmers' consumption power is strong, they can take advantage of the gap after foreign pressure to share a piece of the pie. Now most of the farmers across the country are starving on their stomachs. Where is the consumption power to enjoy industrial products? The smaller the sales, the more forceful the foreign goods (including imports and foreign-owned factories) rush to sell, and the greater the pressure. Chinese-owned factories have no room to breathe. Even if there are no internal diseases, they can only barely survive, where can they develop. Therefore, if the vast number of national farmers, who have the largest consumption, have not been relieved slightly, then light industry is an incurable disease. We see that the Cotton Industry Control Association has been doing its best to think of ways for yarn factories for more than two years, but yarn factories are still sinking and are getting worse year by year. I don't know if those who are talking about industrialization now have investigated the current situation of factories. Just saying that England is like this and the United States is like that is like drawing cakes to satisfy hunger, which is completely irrelevant. To industrialize, we must start with heavy industry, light industry is useless. However, the existing light industry has invested a lot of money, and there are also a lot of employed workers. For the sake of the national economy, it is naturally impossible to put it aside and not talk about it. While running rural factories, we must maintain the existing light industry. Naturally, we must carefully calculate the production and consumption to prevent them from conflicting and to make them mutually utilize. The maintenance methods are nothing more than control and subsidies, advancing in both directions. Regarding control: (1) Merger and union of capital; (2) Organization of trade associations, must be strong and powerful; (3) Those with too old machinery should be stopped; (4) Those with corrupt management should be intervened and corrected, those who do not violate the law should be punished; (5) Regulate labor and capital, so as not to cause unnecessary oblique disputes; (6) No excessive distribution of dividends is allowed; (7) Rectify raw materials and severely punish the malpractice of adulteration; (8) New factories are not allowed to be added unless necessary. Regarding subsidies: (1) Correct the tax regulations so that foreign merchants do not have an advantage; (The current unified tax rules, cotton yarn rolls, have too few grades, the burden on low-quality goods is heavy, and the burden on high-quality goods is light, which is beneficial to foreign merchants and detrimental to Chinese factories.) (2) Measure and lend funds; (3) Exempt raw material donations and taxes, and reduce freight; (4) Give considerable bonuses to those who are excellent in technology management and pass the exam; (5) Transportation and sales must be extremely convenient; (6) Those who use the power of public facilities (such as electricity from government-run power plants) should be given a special price reduction; (7) ) Industries related to national defense (such as cement, chemical fertilizers, machines, etc.) should be given subsidies. If we do this, the existing light industry should be able to struggle to get out of the death line. However, if the consumption power of farmers has not recovered and the sales of manufactured products are not smooth, it is impossible to move towards prosperity. The problem is not in the light industry itself, and it should be discussed separately.

If my country wants to industrialize, it must establish heavy industry. Steel, gasoline, basic chemical industry, power machinery, hydropower generation, locomotives, and shipbuilding, these must be run with large capital. I advocate state-owned ones, not because I am afraid of capital concentration and merchant patents. In fact, my country's industrialists and businessmen do not have this great courage, and everything is started later, and losses are inevitable at the beginning. The steel and gasoline produced in my country, and the locomotives and machinery made by ourselves, will definitely not be as cheap and applicable as imported goods. It must go through a considerable period of time and several improvements and progress before it can be on par with them. However, we cannot be greedy for convenience and rely on imported goods forever. At the beginning, this debt must be borne by the state. Perhaps we will encounter an opportunity where foreign goods do not come, and we can avoid compensation, which is a stroke of luck. If the country has no capital, it can borrow foreign capital. However, heavy industry is related to the life and death of the country, and foreign capital should not be borrowed for economic purposes. Only bond raising or borrowing machinery and materials can be used. Joint ventures or franchises must not be used. To establish heavy industry, there are thousands of things to do. Of course, we must first organize a committee, network experts and people who are familiar with the domestic economic situation, and first arrange the order and formulate a detailed plan. We don’t need to copy the names of five years and three years. As long as we handle it in stages, it is practical. Under today's international situation, can we be allowed to complete the construction of heavy industry leisurely? The problem is still under consideration. "A country in heaven and earth must have something to stand with." Since heavy industry is an essential element for establishing a country, it must be run no matter what. As for success or failure, we only ask to do our best to deal with it.

If we really follow this path, agriculture and industry will advance together. We only take self-sufficiency as our goal. If there is surplus in production, we will exchange goods with foreign countries. The intention is to improve the living standards of the people, and we must never dump them abroad and compete with others for the market. The disadvantages of commercializing agricultural products have been discussed above. If our production depends entirely on foreign markets, then domestic prices will not be stable, and everything will be involved in the world vortex, which will be chaotic and endless. Moreover, it will arouse the jealousy of others, sell our own labor cheaply, and the absorption of cash and expansion of power by merchants will only lead to imperialist struggles and killings. At the end, there will be a panic, and everyone will only be able to look at each other and be unable to save it. Why should we follow their footsteps? We have absorbed material civilization, and we still want to develop our ideal of great harmony and embark on the road of evolution. We will definitely not follow in the footsteps of others and replay the old dramas of history.

10. Conclusion

I have said a lot. In summary, to improve China's economy, we must think about the farmers, who account for the vast majority of the country's people, and plan methods that are truly in line with the national conditions and the times. Integrating industry with agriculture and rural factories is the main theme of this speech. Vigorously developing water conservancy and studying agricultural chemistry are the key points for promoting the main theme. Maintaining the existing light industry and establishing heavy industry are to take into account the current situation and the basic foundation of the country in the future. However, there are still two preconditions that have not been mentioned. One is finance and the other is finance. Finance is the source of capital turnover, and finance is the key to the country's income and expenditure. In particular, tax policy is closely related to the national economy. These two problems are too broad and too complex. Once involved, they cannot be explained clearly in a short period of time. Let's ask for advice another day. (End)

Commercial News

Zhu Bailu's Eight Characters

— Heaven Creates Me

Zhu Bailu's family precepts, though spoken at great length, ultimately boil down to only two sentences that are the true essence of the precepts: "Know your place and accept your fate, follow the times and listen to heaven," these eight big characters. "Know your place" refers to one's capacity. For example, with a balance scale, your own weight can only be accurate up to one thousand grams. If you try to exceed it even slightly, it's excessive and definitely too much to bear. If you use a weight of ten grams to weigh something that weighs nine grams, you'll naturally feel it's too light and can be increased. But if you add two grams, it becomes too heavy on that side. So, when it's at nine grams and nine decigrams, you can only add one centigram, which is sufficient. Although it may not be stable for a moment, if you patiently wait for one or two seconds, you'll see the difference. If you're flustered and hurried, with hands busy and feet scrambling, sometimes subtracting and sometimes adding, it will never be balanced. "Accept your fate" is like receiving an order. Even a military order can be disobeyed, but the mandate of heaven cannot be resisted. Being born into this world, as a woman or a man, is the mandate of heaven. After being born, parents cannot bear to let you die, so they clothe and feed you, ensuring you exist in this world as a person. This is the order of your parents. Parents cannot clothe and feed me for life, so I find my own clothing and food and use it to clothe and feed my parents. Therefore, I accept the orders of others and dare not resist. This is how a child is to a father, a younger brother to an elder brother, and a subject to a ruler. Even if you don't want to, you can only accept it peacefully. Otherwise, it will be of no benefit to you and even cause harm. Since you cannot escape from the world, it's better to be content with your circumstances. A gentleman resides in ease and awaits his fate. Ease means simplicity. If a person stands on even ground and does simple things, without taking risks to seek luck, then they can live peacefully and without resentment. "Follow the times" means the seasons of heaven. Heaven has four seasons, changing between two extremes. At the summer solstice, yin is born, and at the winter solstice, yang is born. When severe cold and intense heat come, I cannot resist them, so I can only accept them. If I don't follow and resist, such as anticipating what will happen in the future, since death has existed since ancient times, why struggle? Even Shun's parents only followed it, and because of this, he became known for his filial piety. Yao passed the empire to Shun, also because he could follow the times. Heaven created me originally for the purpose of creation. Tilling the fields to eat, drilling wells to drink. The tools for tilling and drilling all come from human creation. If others can create things, but I cannot, I should be ashamed. However, the nature heaven has given me is clumsy and not skillful. I can only use the strength of my hands and feet to avoid hunger and cold. Therefore, I exert my efforts in the fields and wells to ensure I have enough to eat and drink. This is what I should do. As for the fields yielding poor harvests and the wells running dry, I can only leave it to heaven. However, human effort can turn the tide. Rising at sunrise and resting at sunset, exerting effort in the fields, then a hundred acres of land may not be completely barren, and nine families sharing a well may not be completely dry. If they are, then neighbors can help each other to share what they have and lack, which is enough to sustain life. Therefore, all people must have a heart of benevolence. Benevolence means that besides myself, there are others whom I must consider. Therefore, the character for benevolence is actually made up of two people, unlike the character for "big," which is made up of one person. Two people make "big," which also means that the power of more than one person, when two or more people work together, their ability can create things and benefit people, which is no different from the ability of heaven. Waking up at dawn, I wrote this freely, using the fresh air of the morning as a way to calm my mind. Whether it's skillful or clumsy, I don't care.

The rescue team from Aguo shouted: "Heavens! Please stop, we really can't accommodate any more."

Little Western Paradise

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Zhiqian was speaking as he headed directly towards Jia Duocai's house. Wanting to give Jia Duocai a heads-up, he called out "Mr. Jia" from afar. There was a reply from inside the house. He said, "Mr. Jia has gone out with a friend. Who is it?" Upon hearing this voice, Zhiqian's heroic spirit was dampened by more than half. This was Yueying's voice. If he reported to her that his grandmother was eagerly awaiting him and was about to die, he would immediately run out. If he waited for Duocai to return, she might think he had ulterior motives, causing unnecessary trouble. Therefore, after calling out "Mr. Jia," he stopped in his tracks, unable to move forward. Yueying, who was answering from inside the house, hadn't seen anyone come over, so she stretched her head out to take a look. When she saw Zhiqian standing far away, she was also taken aback. However, since she lived in the same house with Jia Duocai and saw guests every day, her demeanor had become much more poised. She wasn't as afraid of men anymore. So, she composed herself, smiled, and said, "Oh! It's Mr. Cheng. Is there something you need?" Zhiqian swallowed a mouthful of air and, feigning a smile, said, "There is something, but Mr. Jia isn't home, so what I have to say..." As he spoke, he scratched his head several times and smiled, "It's nothing really. Mrs. Jia, please sit in the house for a while. I'll find someone to talk to you." With that, he quickly ran towards the back of Little Western Paradise. Sure enough, the old Mrs. Zhu was still sitting under the door frame. When Sister-in-law Hu saw him, she immediately pointed wildly in that direction and said, "He's here! He's here!" The old lady tremblingly extended a finger, pointing in that direction, and, grabbing her daughter-in-law's hand, stood up and said, "He... he... is he here?" (338)

Mr. Yun Tieqiao's Remaining Works

— Gu Yushi

My late teacher, Mr. Yun, whose given name was Tieqiao, was a Continued Academician. His lofty writings carried the Dao, and he was a national-level healer. His students and followers traveled from afar, and Mr. Yun always patiently guided them. I, Yushi, was honored to be in his company, able to follow him morning and night, and personally learn the ways of medicine. He did not consider me unteachable and molded me. He revealed the true secrets of the essence of Chinese medicine, including the study of forms and functions, and the points that should be emphasized in treating patients. The two words "forms and functions" come from the Inner Canon. This kind of knowledge can be called the unique knowledge of Chinese medicine, and very few know it. Contemporary students actually misinterpret "forms and functions" as physical shapes. My teacher's learning had roots, his insights were unique, he expounded ancient meanings, and investigated subtle details. Those who are not well-versed in learning cannot even hope to catch up with him. In his later years, he was particularly skilled in calligraphy. For years, due to a wrist ailment, he could not write, and all his calligraphy was done by someone else holding the brush. When I graduated, my teacher was still writing with a strong hand, and I was rewarded with a seven-character couplet. Unexpectedly, the news of his passing came quickly. Caressing his calligraphy, I don't know where my tears should flow. Sitting and facing his remaining treasures, remembering his teachings, how dare I keep them secret? I respectfully publish them in the newspaper to share with those who appreciate them and to express my sorrow.

Passing on the Marvelous Understanding of Formulas and Insect-Like Skills; Today in the Medical World, There is a Tiger's Head

Miscellaneous Works of the New Autumn

— Shu Fan

Ten acres of white lotus flowers in Taihu Lake, several acres of melons in the desolate Song River. Don't sing border songs to startle Rong Zi, the lotus roots wither and the lotus gets old, don't return home! (Bamboo Branch Song)

Hooking up the dim light of Miluo River evokes distant thoughts, remembering my childhood when I stumbled over rocks on the sedge roots; Now I stand with my hands in my sleeves under the windy eaves, letting sorrow turn into hair.

Dew wets spider silk, moonlight falls into the cup, a mournful wind rinses my teeth, the Taoist newly inscribes "autumn insects are long," letting the souls of singing crickets report their names. (Crickets)

Leaning into the wind, silk is continuously spun at the corner of the eaves, carrying the sun, worms creep and peep into the tile gutters, the spider uses its silk to repay a full meal, pitying their hard work chewing on flies! (Spider)

Royal Incense Faintly Lingering Record

— Originally by Princess Der Ling of the Qing Dynasty, Translated by Qin Shouou

Chapter 20. Struggling for Life to See a Beloved Grandson, Hugging Each Other and Weeping, Remembering Past Events in a Year of Famine, Planting Wheat and Inviting Disaster

Even the towels used by the Empress Dowager for bathing show a general sense of extravagance! The towels are edged with apricot-yellow silk thread, forming a neat border, and the center is embroidered with a delicate coiled dragon of the same color; the bright yellow, against the snowy white background, is truly moving! I think sending these bath towels to the exhibition at the fair would be a fine piece of craftsmanship!

When the Empress Dowager was seated on the low table, the four maids were already busy preparing. The Empress Dowager automatically took off her upper garment, exposing her upper body. Although I didn't necessarily want to admire her body, since it was already revealed in front of me, I couldn't help but take a look; this look surprised me greatly. Because I knew the Empress Dowager's age long ago, I thought that a body of an old lady like this must have no beauty to look at, and all I could see must be just a layer of dry, shriveled skin. Who knew that the Empress Dowager's body was not like that at all! Her figure was originally very beautiful, neither too fat nor too thin, the flesh color was extraordinarily fresh and tender, white and without any scars, and it looked very smooth. This kind of body is usually only found in girls around twenty years old; unexpectedly, I saw it on an old lady at this moment, truly a miracle! At that time, I couldn't help but think to myself, if the Empress Dowager's face could be made to look younger, combined with her such a tender and delicate body, she could surely be selected as the most beautiful woman in the palace. (434)

Biographical Sketches

Mussolini and His Wife

— Ying Dai

Due to the increasingly tense situation in Italy, Mussolini, known as a world eccentric, the creator of Fascism, one of the three major dictators in Europe, and the Italian Prime Minister, has become more well-known to the world. Mussolini is only in his fifties. Currently, in addition to being the Prime Minister, he also serves as the Minister of the Interior, Minister of Foreign Affairs, Minister of Corporations, and Minister of the Army. The burden of political affairs is such that perhaps there is no other prominent figure in the world like him? However, although his work is very complex and busy, he is unwilling to do anything carelessly, regardless of the size of the matter. This spirit is indeed worthy of our admiration.

In his early years, his origins were also very poor. His father opened a hotel in the countryside, and his mother had passed away early. His stepmother was a widow who brought some savings with her when she married his father. Before Mussolini achieved success, he had also traveled to France, Austria, Switzerland, and other places to live a wandering life. When he returned from failure, he had no money left. It was not until later that he went to Milan to edit newspapers and organize praise and support groups, occasionally engaging in praise and support ideology. The Fascist party he now leads was born from the late stage of praise and support ideology. On October 20, 1922, he led 100,000 party members and stormed into Rome. In this coup, he seized political power in Italy, and the Italian King immediately invited him to serve as Prime Minister.

After seizing power, Mussolini advocated adopting strong policies to benefit the people and actively build a "New Italy." Indeed, after he took office, Italy's national strength rose steadily. Originally, after the end of the Great War, Italy's position in the international community had already leaped into the ranks of the five major powers, and now, after Mussolini's improvement, it is naturally even stronger. However, at a time when a depressed atmosphere enveloped the world, Italy was naturally no exception, so the economic situation was also very difficult. Mussolini is not only resolute in handling affairs, but also very frugal in his daily life. Whether it is the furnishings of his home or his personal clothing, there is no trace of extravagance. Therefore, his children also have this kind of legacy. He has a considerable love for various sports, and in winter, he is most happy to go skiing in the mountains. He can drive both cars and airplanes himself.

Speaking of Mussolini, we must think of his wife; indeed, this lady can be considered the most virtuous wife. Although her husband is the Prime Minister of a country, her frugality is still unexpected. The clothes she usually wears are simple and unadorned. If you didn't recognize her face, you would think she was an ordinary country woman. She does not live in Rome but lives in a villa in the suburbs of Rome, and it is even more difficult to get to Rome. In social settings, people have never seen her face. Occasionally, when she comes to Rome, she is in a hurry to leave, and her movements are very secretive, never willing to announce them in advance. Therefore, in Italian newspapers, news about the Prime Minister's wife's daily activities is rarely seen.

In fact, Mussolini and his wife are truly a couple who share hardships together, and they are also half-siblings! Didn't I say above that Mussolini's stepmother was a widow? This widow had a daughter at home. When Mussolini's father was running a hotel in the countryside, a little girl often came to the hotel to help - it was the virtuous lady now! At that time, Mussolini also lived in this hotel, and the two of them grew up together, developing a love relationship. In Mussolini's history, although there is no official biography at present, this may be said to be the most romantic page. After they got married, Mussolini traveled around, initially hitting walls on all sides, but when he returned from failure, his wife always comforted and encouraged him in every possible way. Therefore, Mussolini was able to avoid being pessimistic, not giving up, and struggling forward bravely, finally achieving his current position. His virtuous wife also contributed half the effort.

Grain: Arrival of New Early Rice Causes a Sharp Fall of Three Jiao

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, various sources arrived with only thirty-odd numbers (approximately 6,000 shi of goods). Sales in the market were not frequent, and wholesalers were even more slack. Only a few hundred bags were processed, and the market trend immediately declined. As a result, the prices of thick early rice and thin broken rice all depreciated by about a jiao. The prices of new thin rice like Shenzhong Baige also fell by one or two jiao. Furthermore, the supply of thick new early rice was relatively strong, causing a sharp fall of three jiao. The prices of new pointed rice of various colors like Doyang were also difficult to maintain, following closely behind by a small jiao. Only the changing Yin Yuan had no major gains or losses.

National Games, Day Four: Women's Track and Field Sets New National Records Again; Peng Yongxin's Javelin and Qian Xingsu's Hurdles Break Records; Player Eligibility Dispute Comes to an End, Hao and Xu's Qualifications Revoked

Yesterday was the fourth day of the National Games. The weather was beautiful, and because it was Sunday, the crowds were more congested than on the second and third days, more than doubling in size. The number of people in the track and field area was around 20,000 to 30,000. New national records were again discovered in men's and women's track and field, totaling two items: Qian Xingsu's 80-meter women's hurdles and Peng Yongxin's javelin. Shanghai holds an absolute advantage in the three track and field championships and is highly confident in winning the championships. The women's championship is already certain. The ball game matches are becoming increasingly intense, the martial arts competitions are very exciting, and the dispute over player eligibility has come to an end. At last night's joint meeting of the competition and judging committees, it was resolved to revoke the qualifications of Shanghai players Xu Heng and Hao Chunde.

The Women's Javelin Final: Peng Yongxin Breaks the National Record with One Throw: Fifty Meters Two Seven Five — Ao Huaming Emerges as an Unexpected Star in Second Place, Li Shiming Makes a Cameo Appearance and Takes Third

The men's javelin final was full of talent, and the creation of a new record was expected. Peng Yongxin, the champion of the previous tournament, was determined to retain the championship. After the competition began, most of the players could not cross the 40-meter line, so their throws were not measured. Only Peng Yongxin, representing Beijing, threw beyond 50 meters in one throw, exceeding his personal national record of 50 meters and 19 centimeters. In the second week of trial throws, Li Shiming, Zhou Changxing, Ao Huaming, and others all exceeded 45 meters. In the third trial throws, none of the athletes improved. In the final week, Zhang Lingjia, Wang Xuewu, Guo Jie, and others were eliminated, and those who qualified for the final were Peng Yongxin, Li Shiming, Ao Huaming, Zhou Changxing, Tang Xianzhu, and Wu Huanqing, six people. Peng Yongxin did not improve in the last three throws, relying on his first throw to win the title. The official results and championship were as follows:

(1) Peng Yongxin (Beijing) 50.275 meters (New National Record)

(2) Ao Huaming (Guangdong) 49.86 meters

Men's 200-meter Final: Fu Jincheng Takes the Lead

In the men's 200-meter final, there was a false start on the first attempt by Zeng Rongzhong. The race was restarted. Fu Jincheng, full of ambition, took the lead with a vigorous leap from the starting block. Huang Feilong followed closely but ultimately couldn't overtake him. Dai Shuguo started the slowest and was in last place. After 50 meters, he gritted his teeth and sprinted, moving up to second place at 70 meters. However, he was still about six meters behind Fu at the finish line. The differences between the third-place finisher and the subsequent runners were all within a shoulder's width. He Peigen and Xue Jianqiu were not selected. Fu Jincheng's time of 22.9 seconds was quite respectable. After the competition, Zhang Fakui presented the awards.

In the men's 110-meter hurdles final, eight runners started. Liu Yingjun was surpassed by Lin Shaozhou at the first hurdle, who then maintained the lead all the way to the finish line. Women's 10-meter Hurdles Final: Qian Hangsu Breaks National Record Again

Her Stance Was Particularly Graceful Throughout; 14.4 Seconds, Slightly Slower Than the Heats

In the women's 80-meter hurdles final, there were eight participants. Qian Hangsu was in the outermost lane. From the start, Qian Hangsu took the initiative and led the way. The two Malayan athletes followed closely behind. By the fifth or sixth hurdle, second-place Xu Fengying was already almost a hurdle behind. Qian's posture was graceful, and her hurdling was exceptionally agile. In the final hurdle, she exerted even more effort to sprint and won the championship. Although the result wasn't as good as in the semifinals, she still achieved 14.4 seconds, breaking her own national record of 14.5 seconds. It was no easy feat for the shortest athlete, Xu Fengying from Malaya, to win the silver medal.

Women's High Jump Champion Tang Ruirong

New and Beautiful Style

A Result of 1.32 Meters, All of Shanghai's Famous Athletes Were Unsuccessful

In the women's high jump final, there were over fifty participants. The final took two hours to complete. Famous Shanghai athletes such as Zhu Tianzhen and Rong Shuzhen were unsuccessful. Starting at 1.05 meters, only six people cleared 1.25 meters: Tang Duanrui, He Meiying, Feng Miaoyuan, Pang Yu, Su Bolan, and Chen Zhongfang. When the height was raised to 1.28 meters, Chen Cuifang failed on all three attempts and was ranked sixth. Pang Yu, Su Bolan, and Feng Miaoyuan all cleared the height. The height was then raised to 1.30 meters. He Meiying cleared it on the first attempt, and Tang Duanrong cleared it on the second attempt. Pang, Su, and Feng all failed. The height was lowered back to 1.28 meters to determine the rankings. Based on who cleared the height first, Feng Miaoyuan was ranked third, Su Bolan was ranked fourth after clearing the height on the second attempt, and Pang Yu was ranked fifth after failing to clear the height. The height was then raised to 1.33 meters. He Meiying failed on all three attempts, and Tang Ruirong cleared it on the second attempt. Thus, Tang won the championship, and He won the silver medal. Afterward, the height was raised to 1.35 meters, but both failed on all attempts. Champion Tang Ruirong had a result of 1.355 meters in the Fujian preliminaries, tying the national record. Tang used the American rolling jump style, and her posture was very correct, making her an outstanding performer in women's high jump. She is also a pioneer in the major sports meets in our country. The complete results are recorded below.

Women's Hurdles Finish Line (Wang Kai Photo)

Decisions of the Joint Meeting of the Competition and Judging Committees: Cancellation of Hao Chunde and Xu Heng's Qualifications; Representatives from Beijing and Zhejiang Report; Decision to Allow Basketball Players to Self-Report; Player Qualification Issue Temporarily Resolved

The Competition Committee and the Judging Committee of the Games held their second joint meeting at the New Asia Restaurant yesterday evening, starting at 9:00 PM, to discuss the eligibility of Shanghai players Hao Chunde and Xu Heng. The meeting was attended by 29 people, including Wang Zhengting, Chairman of the Competition Committee, Zhang Boling, Chairman of the Judging Committee, and committee members Wu Yunrui, Wu Cunwei, Yuan Lidun, Shen Siliang, Hao Gengsheng, Ma Yuehan, Qiu Jixiang, Dong Shouyi, Rong Qizhao, and Shen Guoquan. Also present were Chen Jianru, Director of the Beijing Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs, Wang Jianwu, Beijing coach (representing the Beijing delegation), and Zhu Jiasheng, leader of the Zhejiang delegation, and Liu Changhe, leader of the Hubei delegation. The meeting lasted for three hours and adjourned at midnight. The details are as follows:

Two Important Decisions Yesterday: First, Chen Jianru, Director of the Beijing Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs, reported on Hao Chunde's participation in the Beijing preliminaries, and Zhu Jiasheng, the leader of the Zhejiang delegation, reported on Xu Heng's situation. After a lengthy discussion, it was resolved that both Hao and Xu had indeed participated in the Beijing and Hangzhou preliminaries, and their qualifications should be revoked. At the same time, it was also resolved that a notice should be issued to all delegation leaders, stating that any basketball players who have violated the above rule should immediately report themselves. If discovered afterward, the qualifications of the entire team will be revoked. This serves as a warning, and thus the major wave of player eligibility issues has temporarily come to an end. The resolutions passed last night are as follows:

(1) Proposal to cancel the qualifications of Shanghai players Hao Chunde and Xu Heng to participate in this Games; the resolution was passed.

(2) Proposal to immediately notify the leaders of all units that any basketball players who do not meet the eligibility requirements should report themselves. If they fail to self-report, once discovered, even if only one person is ineligible, the qualifications of the entire team will be revoked; the resolution was passed.

Shanghai Team Voluntarily Withdraws: Due to the revocation of Wu Bixian's qualification, the Hubei delegation raised a protest, which also involved the eligibility of Shanghai players Wang Jihuai, Hao Chunde, and Xu Heng. The Competition and Judging Committees held meetings and exchanged correspondence for several days, which was quite busy. It is now known that the Shanghai delegation, considering its position as the host city, and with the aim of settling matters peacefully, and in order to uphold the spirit of the Games and avoid misunderstandings and unnecessary complications between units, had notified the Games beforehand yesterday that it would voluntarily withdraw Hao and Xu. Hao and Xu have also declared their withdrawal to the Games. This spirit is commendable. As for Wang Jihuai's eligibility, it has been confirmed and is not an issue.

The letter from Jiang Jianbai, the representative of Shanghai, and Shao Rugan, the leader of the delegation, to Chairman Wang and the committee members of the Games Competition Committee yesterday stated: "Respectfully, regarding the eligibility of our team's players Hao Chunde and Xu Heng to participate in the Games, the procedures are complete, and there is no violation of the Games regulations. We have checked and submitted the documents for your review. Now, as our team is the host city, in order to avoid misunderstandings between units and unnecessary complications, we are willing to voluntarily withdraw them. We hereby request your attention to this matter. Respectfully submitted to Chairman Wang and the members of the Competition Committee, Jiang Jianbai, representative of the Shanghai delegation, Shao Rugan, leader of the delegation."

Hao and Xu Also Declare Withdrawal: Hao Chunde and Xu Heng also sent a letter to the Games yesterday, stating: "Respectfully, in recent days, the issue of Chunde and Heng's eligibility has attracted attention from all parties, and has burdened the Competition and Judging Committees with meetings and discussions. However, Chunde was appointed by Nanjing as a player representative without his consent. Heng went to Nanyang with the Shanghai Zhonghua Football Team in July and is currently serving in Shanghai, and wishes to represent Shanghai. On October 7, the Zhejiang Department of Education sent a letter to the Games to withdraw Heng's qualification as a Zhejiang representative. We believe that the Nanjing and Zhejiang authorities hastily appointed De and Heng as player representatives without obtaining De and Heng's consent, which has led to De and Heng being suspected of representing two units. De and Heng have been involved in sports for many years and understand the meaning of sports. There is no need to argue about who is right and who is wrong. In order to ensure the smooth running of the Games and the friendship between units, De and Heng are willing to voluntarily give up all competition rights in this Games. Respectfully submitted to Chairman Wang and the members of the Competition Committee, Hao Chunde and Xu Heng."

Li Sen's Starting Posture (Photo by Ye Changlie)

The Truth About Hao Chunde's Situation: Mr. Hao Chunde discussed the truth about the matter as follows: "After graduating from Jinan University, I continued to serve at my alma mater, teaching English, for the past four years. This year, during the summer vacation, I went to the Nanjing Training Corps to help a friend with clerical work. It was a temporary position, as I did not accept a formal appointment and did not resign from my alma mater. During the vacation, I went to the Qingdao training camp for training. After completing the training, I went to Beijing and Shanghai and did not have a fixed address. Although the president of Shanghai University has changed this semester, my position will continue. When Nanjing held the preliminary competition, I saw in the newspaper that I was said to have participated in the Beijing preliminary competition. However, the truth is that this did not happen. I did not register in Beijing, nor did I participate in the Beijing preliminary competition. However, the person in charge of the Nanjing delegation once asked me if I would represent Beijing and promised that if I and Wang Jihuai could represent Beijing, we would receive special treatment. Ji Huai and I immediately refused. Later, the Beijing Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs formally sent representatives to contact me and tried to persuade me to work for Beijing, but I refused. The Beijing Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs directly sent a letter to the Training Corps, requesting to express their regards to me, but it was not allowed. At that time, the Training Corps replied to the Bureau of Social Affairs, stating that I had not been issued an appointment letter and was only helping out in Beijing temporarily. There are records to prove this. As for the Nanjing newspapers' banquet, I also received an invitation, but the invitation did not state that it was a banquet for athletes. It only said to have dinner at the Central Hotel. I did not expect that there was a scheme behind this. When I arrived, I saw that most of the attendees were from the sports community and a few famous athletes from Beijing. I did not sign the guest book. At that time, reporters from various newspapers privately inquired about my situation. I immediately stated that I had already registered with Shanghai and would not represent Beijing. This time, Beijing registered me with the Games without formally notifying me or obtaining my consent. I still have work at a school in Shanghai, so I left Beijing for Shanghai on the 5th. Yesterday, I saw in the special edition of the five newspapers that I arrived in Shanghai on the 9th and participated in the Beijing oath-taking ceremony, which was shocking. The Beijing oath-taking ceremony took place after the 5th. I returned to Shanghai on the 5th, so how could I have participated? This kind of groundless talk and arbitrary insult is really inappropriate. This time, Beijing filed a protest. I originally wanted to present a legitimate reason and let the Games handle it fairly. However, in order to ensure the smooth running of the Games, I decided to resolve the matter by making a big issue into a small one, and a small one into nothing. I voluntarily withdrew from the Games. Since I have withdrawn, I have to explain the facts to all sectors of society. I will remain silent and wait for the Games to investigate and make a fair judgment. Whether I registered or not, please ask Beijing to provide evidence. As for the banquet and the photo, I did not know that it was a banquet for athletes. Also, when the photo was taken, many people said it was okay, it was just a commemorative dinner."

Xu Heng Talks About What Happened: Xu Heng talked about the truth as follows: "I have never participated in the preliminary competition in Zhejiang. On June 29, I left Zhejiang to join the Shanghai Zhonghua Football Team for the South Pacific expedition to Java. After returning to Shanghai, I intended to resign from Zhejiang. When Zhejiang sent a letter seeking my consent, I did not reply. Instead, they put my name on the list. I did not fill out or sign any registration forms. Since I am serving in Shanghai, I am representing Shanghai this time. Mr. Wang Zhengting, Chairman of the Competition Committee, also explained to me that there was no problem. In order to ensure the smooth running of the Games, I voluntarily gave up my qualification."

Retaining the Two Judging Committee Members, Zhang and Chen: The Organizing Committee of the National Games sent a letter yesterday in response to the resignations of the judging committee members Zhang Zhengfan and Chen Kun, stating: "Respectfully replying to your letter of October 12, we acknowledge receipt. The organizing committee held a joint meeting of the Competition and Judging Committees on the morning of the 11th, which was after the city government's banquet. All notification letters were delivered to the city government on the spot. On that day, you did not attend the banquet hosted by the city government. Due to the time constraints, we were unable to send a special messenger to deliver the letters. We apologize for this. Fortunately, the second joint meeting will be held at the New Asia Restaurant tonight (the 13th). We believe you have noticed this notification letter. If you have any opinions, please feel free to submit them for review. We are grateful for your support of this Games. We hope you will do your best to participate in this grand event. In addition to entrusting Mr. Jiang Xiangqing to express our apologies and to retain you on behalf of the committee, we are enclosing a badge for your reference. This letter is sent to Committee Member Zhang Zhongfan and Committee Member Chen Kun. Signed, the Sixth National Games Organizing Committee, October 13. Mr. Zhang and Mr. Chen have agreed and attended the joint meeting as usual last night.

The Wang Sisters, Chunqing (Right) and Chunzhen (Left), Are the Most Popular in the Women's Tennis Championships (Photo by Wang Kai and International News Agency)

Men's Tennis

Men's Singles Second Week Concludes: Xu Weipei in a Thrilling Battle with Xu Chengji; Despite Losing Two Sets 4-6, Little Xu Still Earns Praise; "Left-Arm General" Lin Wangsu Is Unstoppable

The second round of the men's tennis singles tournament took place yesterday. Eight groups competed. Four groups, including Ping, Qing, Ji, and Su, played in the morning at 9:00 AM, while four groups, including Java, Hong Kong, Malaysia, and Hunan, began their matches at 1:00 PM in the afternoon. Among them, the match between Xu Chengji from Java and Xu Weipei from Hong Kong was the most exciting. Hundreds of spectators watched intently. The match between Zeng Duancai, the second singles player from Java, and He Jialiu from Hong Kong was also very competitive, as both sides had equal strength. The other groups were one-sided affairs. The results are as follows:

Beijing Achieves Double Victory: Xie Hua, the first singles player from Beijing, opened the match against Duan Yingshan from Qingdao. Xie took the lead with fierce cross-court shots, winning two games in a row. Duan tried to counterattack and returned two games, making the score 2-2. Xie then added four more games, winning the first set 6-4. In the second set, Duan was exhausted and struggled to cope. Xie won the set easily. Wen Yawen, the second singles player from Beijing, is a rising young star. His baseline serves and overhead smashes are powerful. Chen Gengchun from Qingdao is also a skilled player, but he was outmatched by Wen, who won two sets 6-1 and 6-4.

Hebei and Jiangsu Each Win One Group: Zhang Xinhua, the first singles player from Hebei, faced Huang Shijing from Jiangsu. Their skills were evenly matched, and it was difficult to determine who was better. It was a battle of attrition that lasted two hours before a winner was decided. After each winning their service game in the first set, Huang took the lead twice at 5-3 and 6-5, but it was a fleeting moment. Zhang won three consecutive games and won the second set 8-6. In the second set, Huang was determined to retaliate and attacked repeatedly. He managed to win a set 6-4. However, Huang was exhausted at this point. Although he tried to rally in the third set, he was unable to maintain his strength and eventually lost. Zhang won the final victory with a score of 6-2. Li Dingyi, the second singles player from Hebei, and Xu Cida from Jiangsu had similar hitting styles. However, Li was overweight and not good at running. The match ended in two sets, with Xu winning 6-1 and 6-4.

Malaysia Plays Casually: Lin Wangsu, the "left-arm general" and first singles player from Malaysia, is also a dangerous figure in this Games. He faced Ling Zhiyang from Hunan yesterday. It was a small test, and he did not show his full potential. Ling only managed to win two games in the first set. The rest of the games were dominated by Lin. The match ended in half an hour, with Lin winning 6-2 and 6-0. Chen Qian, the second singles player, has excellent skills, but lacks experience, which is his major weakness. He faced Zhang Jinfan from Hunan yesterday. In the first set, Chen made many unforced errors and self-destructed repeatedly. Zhang took the lead at 3-1 and 5-2. Chen gradually calmed down and made accurate shots. He won five consecutive games, winning the first set 7-5. In the second set, Zhang lost momentum and was unable to counterattack. Chen revealed his sharpness and continued to gain points, winning 6-1.

Zeng Duancai Shows His Colors: Zeng Duancai from Java had not been seen in action since the opening of the Games. It was unknown what his skills were like, but his match was crucial to the outcome of this Games. He faced He Jialiu from Hong Kong in his debut. Those who are interested in this Games wanted to find out more about him, so there were many spectators. Zeng's skills are good, but compared to the other national players, he is slightly inferior. His shots are steady, but he lacks a killer shot, making it difficult for him to defeat his opponents. He Jialiu is a famous veteran from Hong Kong. His skills are similar to Zeng's. He had a good chance of winning yesterday, but he lost due to his old age and physical weakness. In the first set, He served first. Each lost their service game. The situation was the same in the following games. Zeng took the lead at 5-4. Zeng served in the next game and broke the record, ending the first set at 6-4. In the second set, the situation was the opposite. Each won by serving, then Zeng changed his style and took a lead of 5-3. He tried hard to resist and made a last-ditch effort, winning one game. But the situation was hopeless, and he succumbed again 4-6.

Weipei Loses with Honor: National player Xu Chengji had been performing brilliantly in recent days, attracting a lot of attention from the audience. Yesterday afternoon at 1:00 PM, the singles match against Xu Weipei from Hong Kong was scheduled. Xu is also a strong player, so there was bound to be a thrilling battle. Before 1:00 PM, spectators flocked to watch, and the venue was soon full. Those who arrived later stood around the venue, several rows deep. However, because this obstructed the view of the back rows, everyone sat on the ground at the start of the game, even those who were dressed in beautiful clothes, which shows how captivating the match was. Unfortunately, Xu Chengji played very loosely yesterday. His cannonball serves and overhead smashes were nowhere to be seen, which was disappointing. Some said that he would face the strong Wang Wenzheng tomorrow, and he would have to exert all his strength to compete, so he was conserving his energy. He just needed to defeat little Xu, which seems reasonable. Little Xu, as always, did not slack off. Although he knew he was no match, he still tried hard to fight and did his best, which was commendable. His sharp serves and clever drop shots often made Xu Chengji sigh in admiration, and he won a lot of applause, which was something to be proud of.

Chengji Reaps the Rewards of Hard Work: At exactly 1:00 PM, the battle between Xu and Xu began. Xu took the lead and quickly won two games. Seeing that the situation was not good, Xu changed his strategy and repeatedly used sharp drop shots to attack, winning one game. Xu then took the lead again at 3-1. Little Xu chased and tied the score at 3-3. Xu then added two more games with long shots. He won the first set 6-4. In the second set, little Xu still did not improve and trailed 2-3. He then went to the net and smashed the ball, frequently using clever tactics and drop shots to gain points. He managed to win three consecutive games and took a lead of 4-3. But his strength was slightly inferior, and Xu did not dare to be careless. He chopped, smashed, and attacked from all directions. One game after another, he won three consecutive games and ended the match with 6-4.

Lost to Yang Weibin of Guangdong 1-2: The Second Week of Singles Competition Has Ended

Yesterday, four women's tennis singles matches and two doubles matches were held. Except for the doubles match between Wang Chunqing and Wang Chunzhen of Shanxi against Hebei in the afternoon, which attracted a large audience, the singles matches were not noticed because they were held at the same time as the matches between Xu Chengji and Lin Wangsu. Fortunately, Wei Maigu, the second singles player, defeated Chen Xiangwei from Guangdong with ease, winning two sets to console themselves. The results of each group are as follows:

Shanghai and Guangdong Each Win One Singles Match: At 1:00 PM, Mao Yuwen, the first singles player from Shanghai, was struck a heavy blow by Yang Weibin, losing four games in a row. Miss Mao remained calm and unconcerned. Relying on her years of experience, she calmly plotted a comeback. She managed to recover and make the opponent panic and make unforced errors. Mao chased the score to 4-4 and eventually turned the tide, winning 8-6. Judging from the situation of this set, with Mao's calm spirit, it would not have been difficult to win the set in one go. Who knew that she would lose two consecutive sets and fail, which is regrettable. In the second singles match, Wei Maigu from Shanghai easily defeated Chen Xiangwei from Guangdong. Chen's skills were mediocre, and she was unable to strike a blow. Wei won twelve consecutive games with ease.

Coconut Girls: Two Losses

Both singles matches between Nanjing and Malaysia went through three sets before a winner was decided, but there was little excitement. Most of the points were decided by unforced errors. As a result, both groups of the Coconut Girls from Malaysia were defeated and eliminated. In the first group, Huang Shannong from Nanjing faced Lu Suli from Malaysia. Ms. Lu took the lead, winning 6-1 easily. But then Huang Shannong also returned the favor, winning 6-1. In the final set, both sides worked hard on endurance.
