Shanghai Wins by a Hair's Breadth, Barely Beats Shanxi by Three Points

The smoke of war between Hubei and Anhui had just cleared, and the competition between Shanghai and Shanxi was about to begin. Most people thought it would be another one-sided affair. Little did they know, unpredictable things can happen. The performance of the Shanxi team exceeded all expectations. Conversely, the Shanghai team was dispirited and disorganized. It wasn't until the very last minute that they barely managed to secure a victory by three points.

In terms of tactics, the Shanxi team was not particularly outstanding either, but everyone fought bravely and didn't slack off at all. Unfortunately, their actions were a bit slow, and they preferred long shots, which were often inaccurate. That was their miscalculation; otherwise, they could have eliminated Shanghai earlier.

The Shanghai team's performance yesterday was entirely unremarkable, especially their slow movements. Every time they had the ball, they stood like wooden chickens, which angered the fans, who started to support the opposing team. If they had brought Yin Guiren and Wang Nanzhen onto the court yesterday, the result would have been unimaginable. After briefly gaining a slight advantage towards the end, they played cautiously, like 麻雀 (mahjong), trying to avoid mistakes. If they can maintain this until the end of the game, they will face the formidable Hubei team in the second round of the midweek games. This hurdle will likely be difficult to overcome.

During the match, Shanxi forward Li Min scored first, followed by another solo drive straight to the basket, giving them a 7-0 lead. When the score reached 9-0, Shanghai's Lu Zhongen finally managed to clumsily score a goal. The situation remained unfavorable, so they quickly brought Yin Guiren and Wang Nanzhen onto the court. With two long shots, they managed to tie the score at 11-11, and the atmosphere changed slightly. After that, the scores fluctuated, closely following each other. The first half ended with a 15-15 tie.

After the break, Yin Guiren made two free throws, giving Shanghai a six-point lead. Shanxi's Lao Li was indeed extraordinary.

He succeeded with a long shot from mid-court. The difference between the scores remained at three or four points. When the Shanghai defense slipped up, Lao Li seized the opportunity and tied the score at 30-30. Then, they took the lead with 34-30. At that time, there were only three minutes left in the game. The audience cheered for Shanxi, and whenever Shanghai got the ball, they booed. Unfortunately, Shanxi's long shots failed, allowing the opponents to capitalize. Lu Zhongen and Yin Guiren each made a free throw and a field goal, bringing the score to 37-34. Seeing that time was running out, Shanghai focused on avoiding mistakes rather than trying to score. They passed the ball around, stalling for time. Before long, the whistle blew, and they barely managed to defeat Shanxi, akin to the style of the Thirteen Sisters (female archers).

In the preliminary round of the men's volleyball competition, Beijing played against Anhui. It started at 1:00 PM, and the result was a one-sided affair. Beijing decisively defeated Anhui in straight sets. The scores were as follows:

Second Set　Anhui hoped to recover lost ground and at one point trailed by only 9-6, which seemed promising. The front row was slightly more active, but they easily wasted several good balls, which led to their collapse again. As a result, they lost again with a score of 21-6.

Hebei Easily Defeats Jiangsu, A Disparity in Strength, 36 to 4, Guangdong vs. Shandong This Afternoon

In the women's softball championship, Hebei played against Jiangsu yesterday afternoon at 1:00 PM at the baseball field. Hebei, with their elite team, easily defeated Jiangsu with a score of 36-4. Cui Huixian is good at striking and has made three home runs individually, which will be a great contribution to this tournament. All the players who take the field score, and the benefits are equally distributed among all. Their strength is evident. The Jiangsu girls fight bravely and are lively in their attitude, but they suffer from unfamiliar skills and lack of experience. The Jiangsu team was overwhelmed by the overwhelming power and struggled to escape. Fortunately, in the fourth inning, Wan Shouzhen made a hit, occupying first base. Memorial Week This Morning, 8 AM in the Gymnasium, Basketball Time Changed

Today is Monday. At 8:00 AM, all staff and athletes of the conference will hold Memorial Week. The 8:00 AM basketball game has been changed to 11:00 AM. Liu Shishi, a famous Hong Kong backstroke swimmer, was unable to travel to Shanghai with the Hong Kong delegation due to work reasons. Chen Yuhui, a female player, was unable to travel because she participated in the South China Swimming Association. Now that the swimming competition is about to begin the day after tomorrow, Liu and Chen have taken the President Jackson ship from Hong Kong to Shanghai on the 12th. They will arrive this afternoon. Liu holds the national record for the 100-meter backstroke at 1 minute and 21 seconds, which he set during the preliminary round of the 10th Far East Games in 1934. However, Liu's recent results have improved dramatically. His 100-yard time is only 69 seconds, and his 100-meter time is within 1 minute and 20 seconds. In this All-China Games, he and Yang Yaokun and Shi Jinping from Guangdong will have a fierce competition, and it is expected that a new record will be set.

Wrestling Friendship Match, Mongolia vs. Beijing Today

The eight wrestlers from Mongolia who came to the conference have attracted the attention of the audience. The wrestling team will hold a friendly match with Beijing wrestlers at 2:00 PM today, and then compete with Shanghai wrestlers. It will be a sensation.

All Athletes Able to Visit All Venues Due to Team Leader Request

The team leaders requested the organizing committee to allow all athletes to visit all competition venues. The organizing committee agreed that athletics events are open to all athletes, but the gymnasium, tennis venue, and swimming pool have limited capacity, so each team can send one-tenth of their athletes to visit each day.

Great Increase in Ticket Sales Yesterday, Approximately 8,000 Yuan Sold

Ticket revenue from the first day of the conference was 13,200 yuan. It decreased greatly in the second and third days to around 3,000 yuan per day. Yesterday was Sunday, and the number of spectators was slightly less than the first day. Approximately 8,000 yuan were sold.

Interview with Pole Vaulting Expert, Wang He: Breaking the National Record Should Not Be a Problem

In order to interview Wang He, who had twice defeated pole vaulting king Fu Baolu during training in Qingdao, I waited until 6:30 PM after the events ended before meeting him in the Shanghai athletes' dormitory. After I explained my purpose, he opened the conversation and said, "I practiced at the sports ground the past two days, jumping over 3 meters and 80 centimeters. I have been resting for the past four days in preparation for creating an excellent record tomorrow (i.e., today). As for breaking the national record, it should not be a problem." After he finished speaking, I said goodbye and left. Judging by the qualifications of the two pole vaulters, Fu Baolu, who scored points in the Far East Games, should be the winner. However, Wang He now has such strong strength, so who will win can only be determined by their performance today.

Small Ball Exhibition at the National Games Scheduled for the 16th; Hubei Province vs. This City

The small ball exhibition at the National Games, the first being a mixed team from Hubei versus this city, is scheduled for the afternoon of the day after tomorrow (16th) at 1 p.m. at the main stadium. It is reported that the Hubei team possesses strong players such as Jiang Chao, Wan Guorong, and Fu Zhishu, making their strength quite impressive. However, although the cooperation of this city's mixed team may be slightly lacking, the individual skills of its members are all top-notch. The competition at that time will definitely be a spectacle.

Men's and Women's National Martial Arts

Men's and Women's National Martial Arts Enthusiastically Welcomed; Archery and Wrestling Finals Held Yesterday; Athletes from Beiping and Shanghai Shine; Mongolian Wrestling Troupe Performs Yesterday

The men's and women's national martial arts competition was held for the fourth day yesterday. Starting at 9 a.m. at the martial arts arena, the archery finals for men and women were held. The women's group was held first, with the first place going to Wang Jiazhen from Hunan. The men's group followed, with the champion being Wang Fuhai from Beiping. Starting at 1 p.m., the wrestling finals for men and women were held, with interspersed wrestling performances by the Mongolian wrestling team. The results of the women's group final showed that the first place was won by Meng Jianli from Shanghai. It was originally scheduled that after the men's group final yesterday, Chu Minyi would perform Tai Chi ball and stick, but due to the lateness of the hour, it was postponed to this afternoon. The details of the competition and the results are recorded below:

Various Sketches of the Competition

Sisters from Henan Excel at Archery; The women's archery competition began at 10 a.m., followed by the men's archery competition. In the women's group, in addition to Wang Jiazhen, the representative of Hunan Province, who won first place, the second, third, and fourth places were all representatives of Henan Province. According to Liu Pixian, the deputy curator of the Henan Provincial Martial Arts Hall, who came to Shanghai with the team, Ma Ruilan and Ma Ruilian, who were selected for this archery competition, are both representatives of Henan Province. According to Liu Buxian, the deputy curator of the Henan Provincial Martial Arts Hall, who came to Shanghai with the team, the Ma sisters' father, Ma Renfu, was a "Wu Tanhua" (third scholar in the military examination) in the past, and is now the archery coach of the Kaifeng Equestrian Archery Association. He is famous throughout Henan Province, and many people have studied under him. Although the Ma sisters did not win the championship in this competition, the beauty of their posture was the best in the entire army. Therefore, the audience called them the "archery sisters." These sisters will also participate in the hard bow pulling performance today. That hard bow requires at least 200 pounds of strength to pull it open, so even for men, pulling this hard bow is not easy. Furthermore, the Ma sisters' mother, Ma Tianjunying, also came to Shanghai. Before the official start of the performance, she also performed on her own, and many of her arrows were able to hit the target, and her posture was also very good. These sisters are truly worthy of being the children of a military family.

Also, this afternoon in front of the podium, there will be a wrestling competition with the Beiping athletes to determine who is best. The Beiping athletes also have many brave warriors, such as Zhang Wenshan, who is tall and strong, weighing over 300 pounds, truly a hero of today. At that time, there will be a bloody battle, which will be even more exciting. Premier Wang of the Executive Yuan happened to be in Shanghai on official business and will also personally visit the podium this afternoon to watch this strange and rare sport.

Wrestling Performances; Continuous Applause; In the afternoon, the wrestling semi-finals and finals began. First, the women's group held the semi-finals, followed by the men's group's lightweight, middleweight, and heavyweight semi-finals. Finally, the women's finals were held, and the Mongolian wrestling team also participated in the performance. The performance of the Mongolian wrestling team was generally the same. Each group of two would often perform a dance when they came on stage, and their clothes were unique in color and style. Therefore, when they danced, it added a lot of interest. When they wrestled, the two sides would often kick each other with their feet. Because they wore high boots, the sound of the kicks was quite interesting. Their physique was strong, and their arm and leg strength was also very strong. They would suddenly separate and suddenly come together, and their strength was very strong. When they fell to the ground, there was a loud bang, which was exceptionally loud and won the audience's applause. Chief Referee Chu, for the sake of seriousness, personally held a small command flag and directed on the field. The Mongolians showed their respect to him when they saw it.

Beautiful Iron Bull Meng Jianli Wins the Championship; Among the women's wrestling athletes, there was Meng Jianli, a representative from Shanghai, who won the championship with a hundred victories. The first opponent she encountered was Peng Shansi, an athlete from Hunan. Miss Jianli seemed to have no one in her eyes and used her hands to drag her forcefully. Although Miss Peng was dragged around for a week, she was not thrown to the ground. Then Miss Peng raised her foot and tried to hook Miss Jianli with it. Meng was caught off guard and almost suffered an accident. They held each other like this for a long time, and when the time was up, a whistle sounded to temporarily rest and continue the performance. Miss Jianli was even more determined to continue her efforts.

Ms. Wang Jiazhen of Hunan wins the first place in women's archery (Photo by Wang Kai and International News Agency)

The Mongolian wrestling team's clothing is unique. At around 1 p.m., the Mongolian wrestling team, led by the head of the team, Si Jun, arrived at the venue, along with the Mongolian football team players. The uniqueness of the wrestling team's clothing attracted the attention of the entire venue. They had already changed out of their previous day's clothing and put on a set of wrestling clothes. The upper garment was made of black leather, and the collar, cuffs, and chest of the garment were studded with white copper nails in a spiral shape. The back was studded with round white copper longevity characters, and some had Buddha statues. The pants were red or white, and there were patterned designs. It is said that ordinary people are not allowed to touch their wrestling clothes, as touching them can easily provoke their anger and cause accidents. There was also a red and yellow striped ribbon around the neck, hanging straight down the chest. They wore long, high boots. According to a Mr. from the Mongolian Political Council who came with them, wrestling performances are very popular among the people of Mongolia, and there is also a sports meet every year, but its content is very different from those held in China. Its programs include wrestling, horseback riding, shooting, and archery. They do not pay attention to track and field and football teams.

Premier Wang will personally visit today. The athletes from the northern frontier, who have come from afar, have performed so many精(精, used in original text) performances. The general audience is白觀不(白觀不, used in original text). Therefore, today we plan to feast on the performances,神(神, used in original text), and surround and fight the enemy, but Peng was ultimately unable to support it and fell to the ground in defeat. At that time, Peng was already discouraged, and in the third round of the performance, she fell to the ground in less than a minute. When Miss Jianli came on stage for the second time, she faced Sheng Guiqiu, a representative from the same unit. Miss Jianli took advantage of her great victory and dragged her down as soon as she grabbed the corner of her clothes. She fought again, and it was the same. So Jianli succeeded and won the championship. Miss Jianli is from Wujin. She is beautiful and strong, and it can be said that her name matches her reality. She brought a lot of glory to the southerners. She graduated from the East Asia Sports College and was known as the "Beautiful Iron Bull" when she was in school. After graduation, she taught at Shangshang Cai Primary School on Edward Road in this city. Today, she ended her black版(版, used in original text) life and is in charge of household affairs at home.

A Fierce Battle Between Henan and Hunan; In the women's group final, Zheng (name not legible in source material) of Henan and Liu Yingyu of Hunan tore at each other. After a long time, each had one win and one loss, and it was difficult to determine who was better. Then, in the next two battles, the two fought fiercely, and neither was willing to show weakness. They held on for two minutes, and the whistle sounded, temporarily ending the battle. They fought five or six rounds like this, but there was still no winner or loser. All the referees were unable to decide the winner. Some suggested using a　　法(法, used in original text) to determine the winner. Referee 　Chu Minyi　(褚民誼, name partially illegible) for the sake of fairness, ordered them to extend the time once and fight to the death. So the two, even more exhausted, shouted and returned to the battlefield. The two grabbed each other and circled for a long time, but it was still difficult to determine the winner. Then Miss Zheng used her head to bump forward, and actually bumped Miss Liu out of the arena. The spectators all stood up to avoid her. Chief Referee Chu was unable to determine the winner, so he had a flash of inspiration and rushed forward to stop them, saying that whoever stepped out of the arena first would lose. So, a difficult battle was finally resolved. But although Miss Zheng won, she had exhausted her strength and had no will to fight. When she was about to fight Yin Peilan of Hunan, she initially planned to forfeit. After Chief Referee Chu explained the situation, she came out to fight, but gave up and fell to the ground in defeat in less than a round.

Athletes from Beiping Defeat Athletes from Beijing and Shandong; Among the men's group, their wrestling skills were very skillful, and because of their great strength, the battle was even more intense. When Zhang Qing, an athlete from Beiping, wrestled with Long Zhili, a representative from Beijing, Long first took the opportunity to twist Zhang's back. Zhang did not resist, but twisted the corner of Long's clothes and bowed his head to the ground, expecting Long to win. Unexpectedly, Zhang suddenly came up with a clever plan, using his head to push against Long's abdomen, holding Long's legs with both hands, and lifting his body up. Long had already somersaulted and fallen behind Zhang. In the second competition, Zhang still used the same trick, and Long was still caught off guard and fell to the ground in defeat. There was also the fat Zhang Wenshan, who was also an athlete from Beiping. His opponent was Ma Qinghe, an athlete from Shandong. Zhang stared fiercely, while Ma calmly responded to the battle. They held each other for a long time, and it was difficult to determine the winner. When they fought again in the second round, Zhang Wenshan used all his strength to twist Ma's back and lift him up. Ma was unable to stand firmly and was pushed to the ground by Zhang. When Ma fell to the ground, his foot accidentally touched Zhang's big belly. Zhang initially suspected that he had been intentionally ambushed, but after an explanation, he was relieved. After a short rest, they fought again. At this time, Ma tried to counterattack and kicked Zhang's foot forcefully, but Zhang still stood still. He then tried to twist Ma's body, but was also unable to succeed. What was even more difficult was that Zhang was fat and his clothes were small, and when Ma tried to twist the corner of Zhang's clothes, Zhang straightened up, and Ma was unable to twist it. Therefore, after two rounds of fighting, they were unable to make any progress, and according to the rules, Zhang was declared the winner.

Ma, the Tanhua, Recalls the Past

The women's archery athletes from Henan, Ms. Ma Ruilan and Ma Ruilian, are the daughters of Ma Renfu, and Guan Fenlan is his best student. This time, Mr. Ma led them to participate in the National Games. The result of yesterday morning's competition was that the total score of the unit was as high as 25 points, which can be said that there are no weak soldiers under a strong general. The reporter asked Mr. Ma about his origins in the Qing Dynasty. He said that he was from Yancheng County, Henan Province. He studied martial arts from a young age. After he became an adult, he obtained the first place in the "Juren" examination in the Ding You year of the Guangxu reign (1897), and the first place in the "Huishi" examination in the Wu Xu year of the Guangxu reign (1898). He only obtained the title of "Wu Tanhua" (third scholar in the military examination) during the palace examination. He is currently the chief archery coach of the Kaifeng Equestrian Archery Association. He focuses on training in horse archery. Most of the members of the association are soldiers, and so on.

Chu Minyi to Perform Today

The Tai Chi ball and Tai Chi stick invented by Mr. Chu Minyi were originally scheduled to be performed at the martial arts arena yesterday afternoon, but later, due to the performance of the Mongolian wrestling team coming to Shanghai, there was not enough time, so it was rescheduled to be held this afternoon. According to Mr. Chu, this Tai Chi ball and stick was invented in 1929 and participated in the World Games held in Belgium in 1930, winning the highest honor award. The function of this Tai Chi ball and Tai Chi stick is to completely practice the pushing hands method. Because there are two people pushing hands in Tai Chi, now you can use a ball or stick, and one person can also push hands. The invention of this ball is derived from the sandbag, but the sandbag is used for punching, while the Tai Chi ball and Tai Chi stick are used for pushing. Currently, the number of people learning it in industry and commerce is gradually becoming more common.

Results of the Women's Archery Group

(Shooting Accuracy); Only eight women participated in archery. Except for Shi Xiulan from Qingdao, the rest were all from Hunan and Henan provinces. The participating athletes were all capable players who had been selected through several rounds. The distance was 20 meters, and the bow strength was 3 li or 2 li, depending on the athlete's convenience. As a result of the competition, Wang Jiazhen, a female general from the Hunan Martial Arts Hall, won the championship. Ms. Wang has strong hand strength and good eyesight, so she was able to shoot three arrows in a row and hit three bullseyes in a row. She is truly worthy of being a divine archer. Ma Ruilan and Ma Ruilian, two sisters from Henan, and Kou Fenlan, three ladies, are all students of Wu Tanhua Ma Renfu. They are quite skilled in walking archery. Therefore, although the championship was won by Hunan, the total score was still the highest for Henan. The results of the final showed that six people were selected, and their surnames, ranks, unit scores, and so on, are listed below:

Tan Meiguan Performs Bicycle Stunts (International News Agency and Wang Kai Photo)

Tan Meiguan's Bicycle Performance; Excellent Technique

Tan Meiguan, an overseas Chinese from Vietnam, took the opportunity of the conference to return to China to present his skills and perform bicycle stunts. There are 23 types of stunts, and the table performance, using hands instead of feet, walking on the plum blossom piles, and balancing the bike on wine bottles are the most valuable. On a small square platform of less than two feet in size, he actually drove the bike on the platform, letting go of his hands or standing or lying down as if on flat ground. The audience all marveled in admiration. His skill in driving is as skilled as ordinary people playing with bamboo, watching his lightness and flexibility, without any obstacles. It is not possible to be competent without several years of hard work. Our overseas Chinese's divine skill is also worth seeing.

Methods for Presale of Swimming Tickets

The conference announced the detailed methods for presale of swimming tickets as follows. The swimming competition will start on the 16th. There are not many seats, and it is bound to be crowded at that time. The conference has specially ordered the following methods for presale of tickets. 1. A long-term ticket for the swimming pool is six yuan (from October 16 to 20), which will be sold at the following locations starting today: (1) Shanghai China Travel Service (Sichuan Road) and its branches, (2) Shanghai Municipal Bank Head Office (Tianjin Road), South Branch (South City Minguo Road and West Branch (Old West Gate), (3) Ticket booth No. 2 at the conference venue (in front of the West Main Gate). 2. There are three types of temporary tickets for the swimming pool every day: (1) 1.50 yuan (if the 6 yuan long-term tickets have been sold out, then these temporary tickets will not be sold), (2) 1 yuan (these temporary tickets will be sold the day before), (3) 6 jiao (these temporary tickets will be sold the day before). 3. The locations for selling the above three types of temporary tickets: (1) Shanghai China Travel Service (Sichuan Road) and its branches, (2) Shanghai Municipal Bank (Tianjin Road), South Branch (South City Minguo Road) and West Branch (Old West Gate), (3) Swimming pool ticket booth at the conference venue. 4. Shanghai China Travel Service and its branches, Shanghai Municipal Bank and its branches will sell tickets the day before and on the day from 9 a.m. to 10 a.m. (for example, tickets for the 15th will be sold all day on the 14th and from 9 a.m. to 10 a.m. on the 15th). All unsold swimming tickets will be sold separately at the swimming pool ticket booth in front of the main gate of the conference venue until they are sold out.

Sketches of the Tennis Court

The female tennis players from Malaya wear rouge and lipstick, quite like movie stars. The female tennis players from Sichuan wear woolen suits, which are extremely neat and have the air of young mistresses. The players from Beijing, Jiangsu, Hunan, and Anhui are purely rustic and extremely simple.

Xu Chengji and his brother Xu Chengwei's doubles match the day before yesterday was warmly supported by the spectators. After the match, they were surrounded by the audience and asked for autographs for as long as a quarter of an hour. Now that this trend has started, after Chengji and Xu Weipei's singles match today, even more people asked for autographs. The referee Gao Cheng was also surrounded. Ling Daoyang was unable to come down, so he was also trapped, and his anxious state was comical.

The Wang sisters, the tennis flowers of Shanxi, were most noticed by the audience. Before the start of their doubles match yesterday, they were constantly surrounded by "cameras." When the competition started, hundreds of people holding cameras rushed into the arena like shock troops, surrounding the Wang sisters in layers. As a result, the crowd was unable to focus the light, and nothing was accomplished. The two sisters, in a state of shock, took the opportunity to break through and escape.

The tennis competition is gradually becoming more intense, so the audience is growing day by day. Yesterday, Xu Chengji and Xu Weipei's singles match attracted an even larger audience. The bleachers were not enough to hold them, and the head of the security team personally came forward and sent a large number of police officers and dozens of Boy Scouts to the scene to suppress the crowd, and the order was well maintained.

Among the male and female tennis players, there are two pairs who are siblings, and their skills are also outstanding, and they are sure to win the championship in this competition. It can be said that they are a perfect match. They are the Wang Chunqing and Chunwei sisters from Shanxi, and the Xu Chengji and Chengwei brothers from Java. They have been inseparable in recent days and are very affectionate. It is truly a beautiful story in the National Games. Their age, physique, and tennis skills all meet the standards. The reporter sincerely wishes them success.

Many of the female tennis players do not speak Chinese. The Wang sisters from Shanxi are young, and the Wei sisters from Shanghai are from McGuffey. One is because their mother is Western, and the other is because they were overseas students. The female players from Malaya not only cannot speak, but also cannot write Chinese. Most of the male players speak English, so the tennis court has a foreign flavor.

National Competition: Tense Table Tennis Situation; Jiangsu, Hong Kong, Macau, and Shanghai Hold Advantages; Championship Decided Tonight at the Assembly Hall

The National Table Tennis Competition grandly opened on National Day simultaneously with the National Games. Every night from 7:00 PM onwards, matches are held at the Central Assembly Hall on North Sichuan Road near Yokohama Bridge. This year's participants include teams from Tianjin, Qingdao, Nanjing, Zhejiang, Jiangsu, Hong Kong, Macau, and Shanghai, totaling eight units. For days, they have been competing in round-robin group matches. In the first group, Macau and Shanghai emerged at the top, while in the second group, Hong Kong and Jiangsu secured spots in the finals. These four teams boast renowned players and possess formidable strength. Their skills are highly refined, and their performances are captivating. Starting at 7:00 PM tonight, also at the Assembly Hall, they will compete according to the drawn order to determine this year's champion. Each team will undoubtedly give their all in the contest, making it difficult to predict who will win the championship. If Shanghai does not underestimate its opponents, it may have a chance at victory. Tickets are priced at 20 cents and 40 cents. The Study Burden and Teaching Time of Middle School Students (1)

— Yi Ping

Currently, it is generally felt that the study burden on middle school students is too heavy. Middle school students are generally busy with their studies from morning till night, to the point where their health is damaged and their bodies are weakened. Those concerned with education should not ignore the seriousness of this problem, but should conduct thorough investigations and detailed analyses, and engage in research, without superficial observations and erroneous reasoning. Currently, people generally believe that the heavy study burden on middle school students is due to the excessive teaching time in current middle schools. This cannot be said to be anything other than a mistake. Upon closer inspection, the origin of this error stems from roughly three causes. First, it is based on the reports of a few individuals who are not representative. For example, in a recent article in the Ta Kung Pao by a Mr. Chen titled "Save Middle School Students," he cited the words of a certain middle school student and a certain teacher. Drawing a conclusion about the excessive study time of current middle school students and its various harms based on the reports of four or five students and teachers is, inevitably, based on weak evidence. Even if the examples cited are not extreme cases, it is difficult to see any representativeness, except for the author's own insistence on adding the phrase "representative" when citing examples. Second, there is a lack of clear understanding of the system itself. For example, the current middle school curriculum standards clearly stipulate that the total number of hours for high school students' daily classes, self-study, and extracurricular activities is ten hours, within which one hour is for morning exercises and extracurricular activities. However, the author of "Save Middle School Students" insists on saying, "High school students have ten hours of classes and self-study every day, totaling sixty hours per week, and the one hour of morning exercises each day is not included..." This is somewhat akin to "deliberately accusing someone of wrongdoing." Regarding various middle school regulations, anyone with a clear understanding of the true nature of middle schools knows that there are absolutely no morning exercises of such long duration. Criticizing a system in this way, however "sternly," is regrettably not "justly righteous." Third, unreasonable realities are confused with the system itself. For example, the current regulations for junior high school mathematics stipulate four hours per week for the first grade, five hours per week for the second and third grades, four hours per week for the first grade of high school, three hours per week for the second grade, four hours per week for the first semester of the third grade, and two hours per week for the second semester. However, in reality, schools often arbitrarily increase these hours, and by a significant amount. In the article "Save Middle School Students," a middle school student's report is also mentioned, which is the only truly representative example among those cited as "representative" in the article. He said that in his school, there are an average of six to eight hours of mathematics every day. This is a far cry from the regulations. I believe that this student is unlikely to be lying, but the principal and teachers of that school are going crazy. They must be using a "cramming" method to deal with students for some purpose, perhaps for the college entrance examination. Last year, I participated in a tour of various middle schools in the capital to investigate the curriculum. As a result, it can be said that there were almost no schools that strictly followed the regulations regarding the number of hours. In general, they were all increased, and the most extreme had up to forty-eight hours of teaching time per week. This is an astonishing thing. No wonder it makes young people dizzy and causes society to curse middle schools. However, this is an unreasonable reality, and the system cannot be held responsible for it. How can it prevail over it?

Important Information for Quitting Smoking (1)

— Zhang Zhongming

Introduction

Since the entry of opium into our country, the scourge of smoking has spread like wildfire. From high-ranking officials to common laborers, the number of addicts is countless. They are generally emaciated and mentally exhausted. How can such a nation, when facing a nation that forges itself, not fail? As the saying goes, things must rot from within before insects breed. We are clear about blaming others but obscure about blaming ourselves. Why blame others for our own decline?

From the late Qing dynasty to the founding of the Republic of China, people in society, deeply concerned about the increasing spread of the poison, loudly called out and strongly argued against the harms of smoking. However, those in power were constrained by financial difficulties and were unable to fully implement prohibitions. Those below saw the government's procrastination on smoking bans and delayed taking action themselves. Therefore, smoking ban laws were treated as insignificant.

Until recently, since the National Government promulgated a six-year ban plan, addicts have begun to feel the strictness of the law, which is very different from the past. They are now in a state of panic, feeling like they cannot continue like this. They are constantly thinking about effective and miraculous remedies to serve as rafts for the sea of suffering. My writing of this piece is also intended to provide those with addiction with a reference.

Chapter 1: The Nature of Opium

Opium is a brownish-yellow gelatinous substance or powder, belonging to the category of pseudo-alkaline narcotics. It is extracted from the juice inside the capsules of poppy flowers. It tastes bitter and has a distinctive odor. It is soluble in water or alcohol. It contains the most important component, morphine, which accounts for about 12%, as well as other pseudo-alkaline substances. It is produced in the Balkan Peninsula of Europe, Egypt in Africa, and Persia and India in Asia. Recently, our country has also been widely cultivating it. The various effects of opium smoking on the body and mind are described below.

(1) Effects on the Nervous System

Opium is essentially a neurotoxin, so its effects on the nervous system are particularly strong. Those who are new to smoking opium, even in small quantities such as one or two pipes (each pipe containing about a tenth of an ounce), will feel mentally happy, their worries will disappear, and their limbs will feel unusually comfortable. Therefore, scholars often use it to stimulate literary inspiration, and busy individuals rely on it to recover from fatigue. Those in the leisure class rely on it even more as the only mental comfort to numb their bodies and minds. As a result, they lie horizontally on their beds, immersed in the misty landscape of opium. The taste of it is something that outsiders cannot imagine. Young people are easily tempted by opium, and the reason for this is based on this.

However, beautiful scenes do not last, and grand banquets cannot be repeated. The days of mental happiness are when exhaustion is secretly lurking. The effects of anesthesia are limited to a few hours. Once the effects have passed, the fatigue on the body and mind remains the same, or even feels more tired than before smoking. Those who are new to smoking are constantly thinking about smoking again, hoping to maintain their excited state of mind forever. However, over time, they become increasingly addicted to opium.

Once an opium addiction is formed, the smoker's suffering increases day by day. The pleasant emotions of the past gradually disappear. On the one hand, after the nerves have been anesthetized for a long period of time, a large amount of opium is required to stimulate the already weakened spirit. On the other hand, they are intimidated by the power of opium and can no longer control themselves. Therefore, the amount smoked increases with time. Those who can limit themselves to small amounts and not exceed them are extremely rare.

As for the mental aspect, after being extremely anesthetized, abnormal changes also occur. In most cases, the mind is颓唐 (tuí táng, depressed), and the will is wavering. The courage of youth and grand plans all disappear. In severe cases, symptoms such as palpitations and insomnia also occur in many cases.

(2) Effects on the Digestive System

The digestive system refers to the collective term for the stomach and intestines. The intestines are further divided into the large intestine and the small intestine. Normally, food first collects in the stomach. After the first stage of gastric digestion, it begins to flow into the small intestine. In the middle, it undergoes a second stage of intestinal digestion. As a result, the nutritional components of the food gradually transform into nutrients suitable for the human body, which are then absorbed by the small intestine and transported into the blood, spreading throughout the body. As for the fecal matter discharged from the large intestine, most of it is food residue, which has no nutritional value. The ability to propel food from top to bottom is based on the peristalsis of the stomach and intestines. (Note: The term "peristalsis" describes the movement of earthworms. The movement of the stomach and intestines is quite similar, so it is also named after it). During digestion, peristalsis is quite strong. After digestion is complete, the stomach and intestines are calm. This phenomenon can be observed in detail using X-rays. In general, stronger peristalsis often causes diarrhea, while slower peristalsis easily leads to constipation.

Opium has the effect of stopping the peristalsis of the stomach and intestines. Therefore, smokers suffer from constipation. Those who smoke small amounts may have a bowel movement once every two or three days. In severe cases, they must wait five or six days until they can have a bowel movement by using enemas or laxatives.

Originally, constipation is the source of all diseases. This is because the maintenance of human health depends on moderation in diet and regular bowel movements (once a day). If the bowels cannot move regularly, the residue contained in the intestines easily transforms into toxic substances. Additionally, after the intestinal tract is blocked for a long period of time, the descent of food is also hindered. Therefore, smokers are extremely emaciated and lack appetite. Although the reason is due to insufficient nutrition, the effects of poisoning are also related.

Furthermore, smokers often boast that opium helps digestion. In fact, this is not true. Opium has the effect of stopping peristalsis, as mentioned above. Therefore, after smoking, the peristalsis of the stomach immediately stops. With peristalsis stopped, the capacity of the stomach also expands. The so-called relief of bloating is the result of the stomach cavity expanding and has nothing to do with the problem of digestion. This is also something that should be noted.

(3) Effects on the Circulatory System

After the heart is anesthetized by opium, the pulse becomes slow. The blood vessels in the brain and skin expand. Therefore, those who are new to smoking often feel a swelling sensation in the head and heat or itching in the limbs. As the opium addiction deepens, this phenomenon gradually disappears. After prolonged anesthesia, the heart becomes extremely weak. It is often unable to withstand attacks from external diseases, and countless deaths are caused as a result.

(4) Effects on the Respiratory System

The lungs are the organs that first come into contact with opium. All inhaled smoke must first pass through the blood vessels of the lungs before spreading throughout the body. After the lungs are anesthetized, breathing becomes slow and prolonged. Therefore, after smoking, one often feels at peace. Additionally, opium toxins can cause chronic bronchitis. The symptoms of bronchitis are coughing and phlegm, but opium has a cough-suppressing effect, so there is phlegm but no severe coughing.

Common Sense on Ear, Nose, Throat, and Eye Hygiene

— Tang Renjin

(67) Stomatitis

Stomatitis refers to the redness, swelling, and increased secretion of the oral mucosa. In colloquial terms, it is called "heatiness." This is an oversimplified explanation. There are many types of stomatitis. They are commonly divided into catarrhal stomatitis, ulcerative stomatitis, aphthous stomatitis, parasitic stomatitis, gangrenous stomatitis, and purulent stomatitis. They are described separately as follows:

(1) Catarrhal Stomatitis

Page 18

The causes of catarrhal stomatitis are mostly due to thermal, mechanical, and chemical irritations. Or it may be due to occupational factors, or it may be caused by the spread of inflammation from the teeth, pharynx, or nasal cavity. Or it may be secondary to infectious diseases and systemic diseases. Now, let's discuss them separately.

(1) Thermal irritation = such as excessively cold or hot foods. (2) Mechanical irritation = such as sharp teeth and the eruption of teeth. (3) Chemical irritation = such as internal or external use of iodine agents, arsenic agents, lead agents, and mercury agents. (4) Occupational factors = such as inhaling copper powder, hydrochloric acid, and ammonia. (5) Infectious diseases = such as typhoid fever, measles, scarlet fever, smallpox, erysipelas, tuberculosis, and syphilis. (6) Systemic diseases = such as gout, diabetes, uremia, chlorosis, anemia, leukemia, and cancerous tumors.

In addition, stomatitis in alcoholics and smokers is caused by the irritation of alcohol and smoke. Stomatitis in children is caused by failure to clean the mouth after breastfeeding.

The main symptoms of this disease are obvious redness and swelling in the buccal mucosa and gums. Tooth impressions can be seen on the tongue threads and buccal mucosa. Saliva secretion is particularly strong. There is often a thick coating on the tongue and bad breath. The oral mucosa on the outside of the tongue is often white. Sometimes small blisters develop. Once the blisters rupture, they become shallow ulcers. Patients mostly feel burning pain in their mouths, which often makes eating difficult. They also complain of a constant bitter or rotten taste. This is because food and saliva decompose.

The course of this disease depends on the cause. Acute cases can be treated in a few days, while chronic cases may take years to treat. The treatment principle is: first, avoid thermal, mechanical, chemical, and alcohol irritations; second, immediately treat inflammation of the teeth, pharynx, and nasal cavity; third, ensure that the mouth is kept very clean. Rinse the mouth with medicinal solutions. If children cannot rinse their mouths, use medicinal solutions to wash their mouths. All medicinal solutions should be prescribed by a doctor.

Tooth Common Sense Q&A (5)

— Lin Yixian

(Question 22) During the period when deciduous teeth are to be replaced, it is certainly not good to keep them. However, if they are lost several years early, before the replacement period, is there any harm?

(Answer) There are three harms: (1) Missing teeth cause inconvenience in chewing and impair digestion, which affects the health of children. (2) Because there are gaps, the neighboring deciduous teeth or the permanent teeth that are erupting will gradually tilt and move forward, occupying the space. This will eventually cause the permanent teeth that should have erupted to have their position occupied and can only grow sideways or slant forward, resulting in uneven teeth that are sparse and dense, improper upper and lower bite, and reduced chewing efficiency. The harm is even greater than what was said in the previous Q&A. (3) It will shorten the alveolar bone, and the face will become uneven.

(Question 23) As parents, how should they pay attention to their children's deciduous teeth?

(Answer) Children should be taught to brush their teeth to avoid tooth decay. If there are cavities, they should be filled by a dentist. Unless absolutely necessary, they should not be extracted early. Also, pay attention to the replacement period of each tooth mentioned above. When they are loose, they should be extracted immediately and not allowed to remain. In this way, permanent teeth can grow neatly and beautifully, benefiting the child for life. Many parents think that deciduous teeth are temporary anyway and do not protect them, allowing them to be lost early. This is a big mistake.

Section 2: The Growth of Permanent Teeth

(Question 24) After the first permanent molars erupt at the age of six, when do the other teeth erupt?

(Answer) After the first permanent molars erupt at the age of six, the central incisors erupt around the age of seven. The lateral incisors erupt around the age of eight. The first premolars erupt around the age of nine. The second premolars erupt around the age of ten. The canines erupt around the age of eleven or twelve (the lower canines often erupt one or two years earlier). The second molars erupt around the age of thirteen. The third molars erupt around the age of seventeen or eighteen (but these teeth often erupt later).

(Question 25) How are permanent teeth arranged?

(Answer) Counting from the midline inward: (1) central incisor, (2) lateral incisor, (3) canine, (4) first premolar, (5) second premolar, (6) first molar, (7) second molar, (8) third molar. The upper and lower jaws on the left and right sides are arranged in this way. The entire mouth has a total of thirty-two teeth.

Mr. Molière and the Medical Profession

— Song Guobin

I reside on Rue Molière, allow me to speak of Mr. Molière:

Mr. Molière was a great French poet, one of the literary giants of 17th century Europe. He was famous for his plays and poetry. His art of satire can be described as extremely sharp. In light of the charlatan behavior of quack doctors at the time, he used a cold, sarcastic attitude to gradually depict their dark secrets. Many of Molière's works belonged to this category. However, because of Molière's works, society became aware of the dark side of the medical profession at the time. In reality, Molière only depicted quack doctors, but society viewed the entire medical profession in the same way! As a result, lawmakers also took notice! They created many legal provisions related to medicine! In this way, while doctors' mistakes decreased, their courage to provide emergency care and their spirit of experimentation were also significantly restricted!

"Failure is the mother of success. Before every successful doctor becomes famous, who can avoid unintentional mistakes and failures? After each mistake, one learns a lesson and gains experience. The more experience one has, the fewer mistakes one makes! Although mistakes are caused by the doctor's lack of knowledge and experience, the vast majority are due to bold attempts and enthusiastic efforts to save lives. These kinds of mistakes arise from academic and ethical considerations. They are not intentional killings, but rather equivalent to saving someone from drowning. There is no animosity between the doctor and the patient. Why would one intentionally kill them? Reputation is a person's second life. Why would one sacrifice it? Considering reason and logic, does that make sense? Therefore, the word 'intentional' cannot be added to the word 'mistake.' Except for abortion, almost no mistake is intentional. Thus, a doctor's unintentional mistake is an academic and conscience issue, not a legal one! Since the increase in medical malpractice lawsuits in recent years, doctors have become particularly cautious when treating patients. Even when faced with critical symptoms, although they want to enthusiastically and boldly try certain emergency methods, the legal provisions for intentional homicide are vividly present before them. As a result, their courage is diminished! Everyone is being cautious, not daring to deviate from the norm in the slightest. Those doctors who have been sued are even more frightened, with specialized obstetricians not daring to perform deliveries! Specialized surgeons not daring to perform even minor operations! The more obstacles doctors face, the more carefully they defend themselves. If this continues, I fear that in the future, no doctor will dare to treat dangerous illnesses. Alas! Who is to blame for this?

Because Molière's works influenced the French medical profession, I was reminded of the results of medical disputes in China. My rambling thoughts may contain a bit of truth!

Medical Science for Pain Relief (36)

— Li Xing

Addicts who have made up their minds or are forced to quit should preferably go to a hospital for proper and safe treatment. If done at home, it is often abandoned halfway. The principles for quitting smoking and drugs are as follows: (1) Those with strong bodies and less severe addictions can adopt the direct quitting method. (2) Initially, use tranquilizers to replace narcotics, keeping the addict in a dazed state for several days, because the most intense period of addiction is the first few days. (3) After the narcotics are removed, any old ailments that are discovered should be treated immediately with other appropriate methods, never using narcotics again. Most of the ailments during the drug period were originally in the body but were covered up by the narcotics. Now that the narcotics are removed, the old ailments are rediscovered. (4) Those with long-term addictions and very weak bodies should adopt the gradual reduction method. (5) During the detoxification period, some may need stimulants, such as those to strengthen the heart, assist breathing, or other stimulating drugs. (6) The most important task after quitting is to nourish the body. Nourishment methods include nutritious food, special attention to personal hygiene, and taking blood-tonifying and body-strengthening medicines. Now that there are safe methods for quitting, it is time for fellow compatriots who have been harmed by drugs for a long time to turn back.

Analgesics (or Pain Relievers)

This type of medicine occupies the most important position among all medicines, and it is also the type with the widest sales. Worldwide sales are easily over ten thousand yuan every year. It is unknown how many people rely on these drugs for their lives. The raw materials for analgesics are no more than a few dozen, but the types of medicines formulated from these raw materials are numerous, not less than several hundred. The purpose of this article is not to solicit business for pharmaceutical companies, nor is it intended to ruin their business, but to clarify the proper uses of analgesic drugs in scientific medicine, to reduce human suffering and improve human health. All explanations are not based on my own ideas, but are indeed based on expert experiments and writings.

A Brief Discussion of Pulmonary Tuberculosis (70)

— Hu Jiayan

Chapter 12 Treatment of Pulmonary Tuberculosis

Section 2 Rest and Nutrition

Besides fresh air, there are two things that are necessary for treating this disease, which patients should pay close attention to: one is the importance of physical rest, and the other is the necessity of rich nutritional food. The details of both are now described separately below:

Why should patients with this disease rest quietly? We know that pulmonary tuberculosis is a type of inflammatory lesion. The general rule for treating inflammation is to keep the affected area at rest so that scarring can occur quickly. For example, in cases of ulcers or external wounds, doctors must apply bandages and make the patient lie down. Pulmonary tuberculosis is no exception. Therefore, patients must rest quietly so that the newly formed connective tissue can completely surround the lesions to promote successful scarring. This is the sole purpose of quiet rest. Based on this reason, then, the claim that so-called deep breathing exercises and various sports (including the national martial arts generally believed in by the public) are beneficial to patients with this disease is obviously nonsense!

The importance of quiet rest has been described above. Then, how should patients rest quietly? First: For patients with elevated temperature, they should lie down all day. This method seems plain and unremarkable, but in fact, it must be done meticulously. Daily conversations and visits from relatives and friends should be strictly limited. As for writing letters, reading books, deep breathing, meditation, and other things, all are harmful and should be absolutely abandoned. After the temperature returns to normal, it is relatively more flexible, but it should not be done too hastily. It is best to have everything guided by a doctor. Second: For patients whose temperature is not currently elevated, the rules for quiet rest are certainly not as strict as the former! However, in addition to nighttime sleep, there should also be several scheduled rest times during the day, roughly one or two hours before and after lunch and before dinner. Going to bed no later than 10 PM at night, and this must be consistently followed. The intake of fresh air outdoors should also be scheduled every day, preferably lying horizontally in a deck chair. In addition, things like outdoor walks, reading books, and conversations can of course be allowed to a certain extent within a certain range. However, there must be a clear understanding of the patient's general condition and the details of the lesions before deciding whether to allow them. Reading books and newspapers that describe emotions excessively is most inappropriate. Many patients cannot tolerate these various rules of quiet rest; especially if the place of recuperation is very close to their own home, this kind of lonely bed life is almost completely impossible. This requires the patient to have sufficient determination and perseverance to abandon everything and strictly follow the rules. If it is really impossible to do it in one's own home, then there is only one way to enter a sanatorium and have a doctor supervise the implementation; one must not be perfunctory and make mistakes.

For children with progressive disease, it is of course impossible to implement the above-mentioned quiet rest rules in practice, but the principle is exactly the same. In clear weather, letting children sleep peacefully outdoors so that they can take in fresh air is also one of the very important treatments for this disease.

Free Talk

Tolerance

— Lingmo

I happened to go with a friend to see a large-scale wedding. After watching it, the friend suddenly expressed the sentiment that he would rather remain unmarried for a hundred lifetimes. He was unwilling to say the reason for his sentiment, but it was probably because, in comparison, every bride had her weaknesses, and he felt that the hope of finding an ideal partner was indeed quite slim. This sentiment will not last long, because a person may not often have the opportunity to act as such a purely objective observer, and even if he tries his best to maintain an objective attitude and observe carefully, the result may not be the same as the general impression.

People usually think that naturalistic writers specialize in exposing people's weaknesses, but this is really a misunderstanding. Naturalistic works certainly do not have ideal, lovable characters that approach perfection like those in romantic works, but neither do they have purely ugly characters that are so ideal. Although we often feel that the characters in naturalistic works are ridiculous and ridiculed, we cannot infer that the author had a ridiculing intention when writing.

There are indeed writers who specialize in finding ridiculous characters to describe. But they often reveal their deliberate affectation. The Travels of Lao Ts'an and The Scholars both ridicule corrupt scholars, but the village schoolteacher in The Travels of Lao Ts'an only makes people feel that he is a fabricated joke, while the characters like Ma Chunshang in The Scholars are real people. When we see them in real life, we do not necessarily find them funny until they are written about. The difference between the reader and the author is only because the author's observation is more complete, not because the author is better at discovering their ridiculousness. From today's perspective, Yu Yude is almost as ridiculous as Ma Chunshang, but the author probably never intended Yu Yude to become an object of ridicule. However, since he was drawn as a model, every model inevitably has its ridiculousness.

A person's character always combines shortcomings and strengths. If the author can truthfully write about their shortcomings without exaggerating them, then he must also truthfully write about their strengths. Whether a work can have this tolerance often reveals whether its ridicule is malicious. Great writers generally do not write with malice. A friend once talked to me about Zola. He believed that Zola's greatness lies in his generosity. I have not read many of Zola's works, so I certainly do not understand this sentence very well. But if L'Assommoir and Nana can be regarded as representatives of Zola's works, then this statement is quite credible.

I always liked Chekhov's play The Seagull very much. What caught my attention the most was Philan, the expatriate. Although that person was degenerate, depressed, and almost beyond redemption, he was also quite clever and insightful, making people still feel that he was lovable. Such people are commonly seen in Western works and are also very common in Chinese society, but it seems that few people write them into their works.

From what I have seen personally, Old Man Ding in Divorce can be said to belong to this type. This book can be said to end with the miracle done by Old Man Ding. This miracle is inevitably a bit abrupt, but the thorough human touch of Old Man Ding is fully revealed even before the success of this miracle. The author of Divorce is very fond of exploring human touch, but the human touch of characters like Brother Zhang is always covered by his humor, while it is contrasted very clearly in Old Man Ding.

From Old Man Ding, one can easily think of Kong Yiji. The proper ending for this person is probably just like Kong Yiji. Whether or not a little brilliance should be painted on Kong Yiji's image is naturally a question, but if we feel that the treatment of Kong Yiji is already different from the treatment of Ah Q, then we may as well say that the author had a more generous tendency when writing Kong Yiji.

Singapore Port (Part 1)

— Liu Ming

——A Record of Returning from the South——

When the ship arrived at the dock in Singapore, the passengers had to flock ashore to buy things or visit the nearby attractions. Only those unemployed workers who were being sent back to their country and a few prisoners being deported remained on board, watched over by the local police.

The pockmarked young man, who had been sleeping in the hold, had been deported for breaking the law. As soon as the ship stopped, he opened his eyes and climbed onto the deck. Seeing the streets, buildings, and coconut groves in the distance bathed in the scorching sun, seemingly glowing, he raised his hands and shouted happily:

"Heh heh, Singapore!"

According to his old habits, he was about to wave his hands a few more times, but suddenly he saw the Malay devil in uniform standing proudly on the railing, staring at him, so he gently lowered his hands and stopped speaking.

Just then, the middle-aged fat merchant opened his umbrella and walked towards the escalator leading to the dock. Seeing this situation, he tilted his head and glanced at the young man who often spouted literary phrases on the way, as if gloating, and deliberately said loudly:

"Let's go ashore. Don't you want to take a look? You're strange. We'll be stopping for half a day. Are you going to sit here and be imprisoned?"

The young man had been leaning against the ship's railing, gazing at the shore. Hearing him call out, he followed him. When they arrived at the dock where rice bags and coconuts were being transported, the middle-aged fat merchant turned his head and glanced at the ship, with a mocking look on his face.

The pockmarked young man silently spat on the ground below, then immediately turned back, showing an expression of disdain.

Over there, the old man was sitting diagonally, wrapping his bare feet with old felt. He used knowing eyes to point out some of the towering buildings, clock towers, and Flagstaff Hill to the Burmese woman and child beside him, as if introducing old friends. Like the pockmarked young man, he was being deported for breaking the law, and he had his family with him.

Next to them, street vendors were selling noodles and clam soup that had just been brought on board. Some of the passengers who had not gone ashore were eagerly buying and eating, and the scene was very lively.

The pockmarked young man walked over and seriously shouted:

"Old man, my treat."

"Really?"

The old man put down the hand he had been using to point out the sights on the shore and used it to scratch his waist instead, asking with a look of disbelief,

"Aren't you hungry? ... Who's trying to fool you?"

After the pockmarked young man said this seriously, he swallowed a big gulp of saliva.

The old man had long been disturbed by the atmosphere of people eating snacks around him. Seeing that the pockmarked young man didn't seem to be joking, he glanced at the steaming clam soup, licked his lips, and said:

"Okay, don't treat us to anything else, just a few bowls of clam soup!"

He also handed a bowl to his little child, who sniffled.

"Bah, what's the point of eating clam soup? ... If I'm going to treat, I'm going to treat you to something good. Let's go!"

Standing on a Line

On the Beach

— Nanyun

Arrived in Tokyo on July 15th. The weather was unexpectedly hot.

Life was very difficult—couldn't speak Japanese well, especially couldn't understand it. I had studied it in extra classes in my home country, but unexpectedly, apart from a little grammar that I could grasp, the training of my mouth and ears was equal to nothing.

A few friends who had arrived in Japan before me were going to the beach, so I went with them.

Beach life is happy. There is a cool breeze in the morning; beautiful sunsets in the evening; and sometimes a bright moon. Although it is very hot during the day, with the ocean lying beside you, you can jump into its embrace and all the heat will disappear, leaving you feeling comfortable and content.

Unfortunately, it often rains. At this time, you really feel bored. The sea is visible but inaccessible. The mountains stand with a sad and bleak look. Unable to bear the boredom, I had to play games with the landlord's children, play Go, flick beans, and learn a few children's songs from them.

Sometimes I also went to chat with a few Chinese friends on the beach.

There are no restrictions on chatting. It can go from east to west, from south to north. It can also go from ancient to modern, from modern to ancient. If you want to say that "words are the voice of the heart," then this "word" often does not refer to a person's solemn speech, but is somewhat close to the boring nonsense during chatting.

Occasionally, we talked about the death of a female classmate.

A friend said: "The two sisters looked too different. The younger sister was so beautiful, the older sister was so ugly. If the younger sister had died, that would have been a pity. If the older sister had died, that wouldn't have been anything."

He was studying economics. He said this, and I didn't want to argue. Society has determined people's intentions. In a male-centered private property system, beauty is a condition for a woman's survival. This is almost the case in the hearts of most men.

But I remembered what he said two days ago:

"The female shop assistants in the company are simply like machines, unable to have any free will. In capitalist society, living people can be used as machines, and machines can also be used as living people."

At that time, I felt his words were very sharp.

If chatting really expresses a person, then isn't the exaggeration of theory like a radio? This is what is called:

Books can sometimes influence people, but the power of historical society will overflow from people, growing into a latent consciousness.

Now I have returned to Tokyo for more than a month. Today is Sunday, and it happens to be raining. Sitting alone at my desk, listening to the sound of rain, I suddenly remembered the words of my friend on the beach.

When will women be able to get rid of the conditions of beauty and ugliness and have their value determined by their ability to perform?

I hope the answer to this question can resonate in the hearts of all women who are oppressed by evil forces!

Thoughts on Visiting the Garden

— Tang Tao

Because it was a Sunday, I was browsing in the old bookstore at the City God Temple, and happened to find that the inner garden was open, so I went for a stroll. This place is not very big, but it took me an hour to walk around it. What's the reason?! It's because it was crowded.

Crowding is the best skill of Chinese people. The "ladies" who visited that day had developed this inherent culture quite a bit. But what made me stay for so long was not entirely this, but rather because the garden paths were winding, spiraling, and narrow. The toes of the people behind were touching the heels of the people in front, winding and turning. At times, I couldn't breathe—but I still had to squeeze.

This problem is said to be because it was originally a private garden.

But there are also several private gardens owned by foreigners in Shanghai, which are mostly bright and spacious, with flower branches in neat rows and whole pieces of grassland, where you can walk and run. However, these are Western-style, or rather, Europeanized. Ours, however, is really very refined, planting a few stalks of slender bamboo, planting a banana tree, or digging a lotus pond and building a rockery that almost occupies the entire garden. So it is winding, spiraling, and narrow. Is this to teach oneself or the children the ability to climb mountains in preparation for exploring the Himalayas? It's not. In fact, it is to keep a model of landscapes, to show one's yearning, to show some elegance, and to let the children imitate it, so that they can stroll leisurely, travel in mountains and rivers, and be an elegant scholar in the future.

We are really followers of the doctrine of propriety.

Therefore, if we drink tea, it is mostly bitter tea; when we write articles, we advocate the tranquility of autumn, but we are not very enthusiastic about the vigor of spring. But if we say that this is approaching old age and having a premonition of decline, it is not entirely true. These sighing and lamenting people are actually young people around thirty years old, who can't be said to be old or declining. Their predecessors left behind a winding, spiraling, and narrow environment. They walk leisurely, fiddle with their sleeves, and sway back and forth. They grew up in this inner garden-style society and are used to it.

But can we only get used to it forever?

The answer is: yes. If the inner mechanism does not change, it is not easy to change everything in the inner garden. The inner garden in the city has been renovated, but because it is necessary to maintain its original appearance, it is still winding, spiraling, and narrow, and you can't see any new atmosphere at all. To change this "habit," there must be sacrifices. Removing the rockery in front of you and filling in the lotus pond will create a fresh grassland that is bright, spacious, and where we can walk and run.

After visiting the inner garden, I wanted to write a record, but it is still just a few thoughts.

Honorable Old Woman (6)

— Jiang Maoxiu, translated by Ren Jun

As the war continued to bring victories, the number of deaths and injuries only increased day by day. The initial cheers of joy had now taken on a tragic color. Government officials, military veterans, and elementary schools and other consolation personnel could not help but be active every day, busy with visiting bereaved families. And everything was covered up by the two words "honor." In reality, if you had not lived in that kind of atmosphere, you might not be able to imagine how much magic the two words "honor" had at that time. No matter how pitiful the bereaved family was, people used the two words "honor" to comfort them.

From this time on, the rice-cooking old woman inexplicably became gloomy and contemplative, and looked completely different from her previous state. When people were talking about the war, she seemed to try her best to avoid listening to it. Needless to say, she had come to realize that the deaths or injuries that had always seemed to have nothing to do with her were no longer other people's business. It was because her own son was also fighting in Lushunkou.

She became even more superstitious than before. She ran to all the temples and shrines in the city to worship, almost like a fanatic.

"Namo Amitabha, Namo Amitabha."

She constantly chanted the Buddha's name while doing chores. Moreover, people heard her muttering to herself in the kitchen, looking very focused, while washing rice or starting a fire:

"Buddha! God! I only have one son. Please protect his life! Please take my old life to replace my son's. Please, please help me, Buddha! God! You are a kind person, you know how much I cherish my son. Bless, bless, Buddha! God!"

At this moment, the tears flowing down her nose were shining like water droplets.

Sometimes, she would suddenly make a fuss. As soon as she met someone, she would grab them, no matter who they were, and splash with saliva, saying such things to you:

"Look, people are going to die sooner or later anyway. You and I are going to die too, and my son will have to die sometime sooner or later. Anyway, we all have to die, so it's better to die in the war. Because that's an honorable death. — That's what I think. Isn't it? Huh?"

In her shining, crazy eyes, it seemed that you could see the kind of infinite suffering that was being forcibly suppressed. No matter who saw her eyes, they would deeply sympathize with her. People gently accepted her words and slowly comforted her.
